=== PAGE 5 ===
Referral Marketing
Referral Marketing helps your brand run referral programs with evergreen and time-bound promotions
for your customers. Marketing managers can design and launch referral promotions within minutes.
Referral Marketing takes care of the rest with its inbuilt automations. The inbuilt automations track
referrals across their complete lifecycle, send targeted marketing emails, and reward brand advocates
and their referred friends. After the launch, marketing managers and business executives can track the
performance of the referral program by using prebuilt CRM Analytics dashboards.
To try the capabilities of Referral Marketing hands-on, get a Referral Marketing trial org.
Watch this video to understand how Salesforce Referral Marketing works.
Watch the video: https://play.vidyard.com/9HXuA6dzrm2TgTEjiRuJLy
If you aren’t able to watch the video in full screen, open the video in a new tab: How Salesforce
Referral Marketing Works.
Learn About Referral Marketing
Learn about the key terms and roles in Referral Marketing. Explore the Referral Marketing data model
and the referral program workflow.
Design a Referral Program
Marketing managers can design a referral program and its promotions by completing a few simple
steps in the Referral Marketing app.
Configure Referral Processes
After marketing managers create the referral program and add its promotions, the admin or the
developer can configure the everyday processes. The processes include advocate enrollment, activity
tracking, and voucher redemption.
Manage a Referral Program
After advocates join the brand’s referral promotion and start referring their friends, marketing
managers can track the progress of each referral.
Get Predictions about Advocates’ Likelihood of Referring
Use Scoring Framework to get predictions about the likelihood of advocates referring their friends. Use
these scores to pursue the right members with the right promotions. Increase your customers, control
the customer acquisition cost, and reduce your contacts’ displeasure with being pursued by focusing
on advocates with higher referral likelihood scores.
Get Predictions about Non-Advocate Contacts’ Likelihood of Referring
Use Scoring Framework to get predictions about the likelihood of non-advocate contacts referring
their friends. Use these scores to pursue the right contacts with the right promotions. Increase the
number of your customers, control the customer acquisition cost, and focus on contacts with higher
1

=== PAGE 6 ===
Referral Marketing
referral likelihood scores.
Work with Referral Marketing Analytics
The Referral Marketing Analytics app provides insights into the performance of your referral programs
based on referral data, advocate participation, referral conversion, and promotion revenue.
Build Solutions Based on Your Requirements
Every company has their own business needs and marketing strategies. Referral Marketing is flexible
and you can extend it to meet your business needs. Review these common solutions that you can
build with Referral Marketing.
Manage Data Protection and Privacy for Referral Marketing
When brands run their referral programs, they must comply with local and global data protection and
privacy regulations. As part of your brand’s referral program strategy, decide how you want to delete,
export, archive, restrict access, manage consent, and restrict the processing of customer data stored as
part of the referral programs.

Advocate
A person who refers or is willing to refer their friends to your brand
Friend
A person referred by an advocate.
Extended Reward
A tailored referral reward that's used to incentivize the advocate and their referred friend to join a
referral promotion. You can offer rewards like payout commission and gift cards.
Referral
A record that tracks the status of a referral that an advocate shares for a friend.
Referral Program
A program to manage and track the advocate referrals.
Voucher
A reward that’s provided to advocates and their friends.
Promotion Template
A reuseable template that's used to create similar promotions.
Referral Promotion
A referral program can consist of multiple promotions. You can create referral promotions that
are evergreen or time-bound.
Transaction Journal
A record that tracks an activity of an advocate or of their referred friend.

Learn about the objects in the B2C Referrals data model.

Objects to Design a B2C Referral Program
Use these objects to create a B2C referral program and its promotions.
Loyalty Program
Stores information about referral programs.
Voucher Definition
Stores information about voucher templates that are used to issue vouchers to advocates or to
their referred friends. Each voucher definition is associated with a referral program.
Promotion Template
Stores information about the reusable referral promotion templates that are used to create
promotions.
Promotion Stage Template
Stores information about the stages of a promotion template. A promotion template's associated
6

=== PAGE 11 ===
Referral Marketing Learn About Referral Marketing
promotion stage templates contain information on when advocates and their referred friends
are rewarded and the activities that rewards are offered for.
Promotion
Stores the configuration and detailed information of referral promotions. Each promotion is
associated with a referral program.
Promotion Stage
Stores information about the stages of referral promotions.
Email Template
Stores the content of the marketing emails that are sent to advocates and to their referred
friends for referral promotions.
Promotion Stage Email Template
Stores information about email templates that are used to send marketing emails to advocates
and to their referred friends at each promotion stage.
Loyalty Program Widget
Stores the details of a referral promotion’s widget.
Segment
Stores information about a Data 360 segment. This object is available in orgs where Data 360 is
enabled.
Promotion Market Segment
Stores information about the Data 360 segment that consists of referral promotions’ target
audience. This object is available in orgs where Data 360 is enabled.
Campaign
Stores the details of a campaign that consists of a referral promotion’s target audience.
Internal Organization Unit
Stores the details of a Marketing Cloud Engagement business unit’s connection with Referral
Marketing. Referral promotions are associated with a connected business unit. The marketing
journeys and emails of the promotion are automatically created in the associated business unit
when you activate the promotion.
Loyalty Program Engagement Attribute
Stores the details of a referral promotion’s reward limit or daily referral limit for advocates.

Objects to Run a B2C Referral Program
Use these objects to run a B2C referral program and its promotions.
Contact
Stores information about an advocate or referred friend.
Loyalty Program Member
Stores information about an advocate.
8

=== PAGE 13 ===
Referral Marketing Learn About Referral Marketing
Loyalty Program Member Promotion
Stores information about the referral promotions that advocates have joined. The count of active
Loyalty Program Member Promotion records associated with active referral promotions
determine the count of active advocates in the org.
Referral
Stores information about each advocate referral. Each referral contains the details of the
advocate who referred their friend and of the referred friend.
Transaction Journal
Stores information about the activities of advocates and of their referred friends.
Journal Type
Stores information about the type of referral activities that you create transaction journals for.
Referral Marketing provides a journal type named Referral out-of-the-box and you can use it to
track all referral activities. You can’t extend or customize the Journal Type object or the Referral
journal type.
Journal Subtype
Stores information about the subtype of referral activities that you create transaction journals for.
Voucher
Stores information about the vouchers that are issued as referral rewards to advocates and to
their referred friends.
Product
Stores information about the product that a referred friend purchased.
Product Category
Stores information about the product category that a referred friend purchased a product from.
Loyalty Program Member Attribute Value
Stores information to track an advocate’s progress towards reaching their referral promotion’s
reward limit or daily referral limit.
See Also
Referral Marketing Developer Guide: Referral Marketing Standard Objects

Marketing managers in your company can decide when advocates and their referred friends are
rewarded. You reward the advocate or their friends only one time during the referral journey. For
example, you can reward an advocate when they refer their friends and reward advocates for signing up
with the brand. You can't reward advocates and their friends again after friends complete an activity.

Considerations for Referral Marketing Implementation
When you plan your brand’s Referral Marketing implementation strategy, you must account for certain
key considerations.

Person Account
Referral Marketing uses both contacts and person accounts to store information about advocates and
their referred friends. Before you implement Referral Marketing in your company's org, we recommend
you to set up Person Accounts.
If you have a limitation on setting up person accounts in your org, you can still implement Referral
Marketing. The process of enrolling advocates and tracking referral activities differs from the standard
11

=== PAGE 16 ===
Referral Marketing Learn About Referral Marketing
procedure. For more details, refer to these sections:
•
Advocate Enrollment Without Person Account
•
Referral Activity Tracking Without Person Account
Active Advocate Count
With the Referral Marketing license, your brand can have 100,000 active advocates. An active advocate
represents a customer’s active engagement with an active referral promotion. The active advocate count
denotes the number of customers that the brand is actively engaging through their referral promotions.
Salesforce considers an advocate as active only when:
•
The promotion that the advocate is a part of is active
•
The Loyalty Program Member Promotion record that associates an advocate with a promotion is
active.
If a customer is an active advocate of two active referral promotions, then the active advocate count of
the customer is two. If a customer is engaged in multiple promotions, then each promotion engagement
is counted as one active advocate.
Tip To onboard more than 100,000 active advocates, inquire with your company’s Salesforce rep
about additional advocate packs.
Example Here are a few examples of how the active advocate count is calculated:
Business Scenario Active Advocate Count
A brand has three promotions, two are active and 40,000 (27,000 plus 13,000)
one is inactive. Among the two active promotions,
one has 27,000 active advocates and the other
has 13,000 active advocates. The inactive
promotion has 6,000 active advocates.
A brand has two active promotions. In one 82,250 (65,250 plus 17,000)
promotion, there are 65,250 active advocates and
500 inactive advocates. The second promotion
has 17,000 active advocates and 720 inactive
advocates.
A brand starts off with two active promotions. The 2,500 (1,500 plus 1,000)
two promotions have 1,500 and 1,000 active
advocates. 200 customers join each promotion as
advocates.
A brand has one active promotion and adds 500 700 (500 plus 200)
customers to the promotion as active advocates

Referral Marketing APIs
To integrate your referral program with external systems, use the set of business APIs available with
Referral Marketing. The number of times that you run the Referral Marketing APIs count against your
Referral Marketing org’s API limits.
Key Considerations for Marketing Cloud Engagement
Area Consideration
Super Messages Referral Marketing sends emails to a referral
program’s advocates and their referred friends by
using journeys in Marketing Cloud Engagement.
When marketing managers design referral
promotions, they finalize the emails that they send
to advocates and friends. The emails that are sent
for referral programs and their promotions count
against your Super Messages count in
Engagement.
Connection Before marketing managers create and run referral
promotions, the admin must set up the
connection between Referral Marketing and the
brand’s Engagement business unit. Without the

Journey Customizations After marketing managers activate a promotion,
journeys are created in the brand’s connected
Engagement business unit. An Engagement user

to send mobile notifications or WhatsApp

Profile Center Link in Emails
Referral promotion emails that are sent using
Marketing Cloud Engagement don't include the
link to Profile Center by default and marketing
managers can't activate promotions when the
Profile Link Check setting is turned on in
Marketing Cloud Engagement.
To include the Profile Center link in referral
promotions, edit referral promotion email
templates and add the required Profile Center
details.

Object Permissions for B2C Referrals
B2C Referrals comes with a set of objects to view and manage referral programs. Admins must provide
role-specific object access to users in the org. For example, marketing managers need permission to
view, create, and edit referral programs and their related records whereas admins need access to delete
records as well.

Tip The standard System Administrator profile comes with read, create, edit, delete, view all records,

Referral Marketing object access.

Permission to Create Target Audience for Promotions
Use Referral Marketing to target promotions towards specific customer groups. Filter contacts in the org
by using Data 360 segments or campaigns. Provide marketing managers the permission to create
segments and campaigns in the org.

Set Up Communicaion Method
You can configure how you communicate with advocates and their friends throughout various stages of
the promotion journey. Follow the data protection and privacy policies of your region and obtain the
required consent from the target audience.
Note Any new referral promotion that you create will be based on your org's current preference for
content distribution.
When you change your org's communication method, existing referral promotions continue to use the
option they were originally configured with. For example, if a referral promotion was created with
Marketing Cloud Engagement enabled and you later switch to Marketing Cloud, the promotion
continues to work using Marketing Cloud Engagement distribution.
Learn About Communication Methods
You can configure the communication method according to your business requirements on the Referral
Marketing Settings page, accessible under Setup.

friends don't receive referral emails.

Data 360 Segment-Based Referral Promotion Audience Segmentation
Typically, marketing managers design referral promotions that target specific customer groups. Advocates
of your company's referral promotions are categorized into customer groups by using Data 360 segments
and campaigns. The segments can be a part of any Data 360 companion org. If marketing managers
want to use Data 360 segments as the target audience for promotions, admins determine how to verify
whether advocates are part of a promotion's segment.
Ways to Verify Advocate's Data 360 Segment
When advocates try to join a referral promotion, there are ways to verify whether the advocate belongs to
the promotion's eligible Data 360 segment. Companies can verify whether an advocate belongs to the
promotion's eligible segment using either Data 360's Query API or using data graphs.
Note You can select members from Data 360 segments across multiple data spaces. For best
results, select your promotion's target audience from segments found within one data space.
Find an Advocate's Segment with Data Graph
Use prebuilt data graphs to check whether an advocate belongs to a referral promotion's eligible
segment if your company expects a high volume of advocates to join referral promotions simultaneously
throughout the day.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing and
Data 360

=== PAGE 34 ===

Install the Referral Marketing Data Graph Unmanaged Package
Referral Marketing provides an unmanaged package named Customer Engagement Data Graphs. You
can install the package from here.
Create Data Graphs from the Referral Marketing Data Kit
A data kit is automatically added to your org after you install the Customer Engagement Data Graphs
unmanaged package. Use the data kit to create these data graphs:
•
Individuals for Customer Engagement—Enables the Referral A Friend widget and the Referral Advocate
Enrollments API to out whether an advocate is part of the promotion's eligible Individual-based
segment.
•
Loyalty Members for Customer Engagement—Enables the Referral A Friend widget and the Referral
Advocate Enrollments API to out whether an advocate is part of the promotion's eligible Loyalty
Program Member-based segment.
After the data kits are created, ensure that you save and run them.
See Create a Data Graph from a Data Kit.
Create Data Graphs from Scratch
You can opt to create the data graphs that are used to find customers' segments on your own. Here's
what you must do to ensure that the data graphs can be used to find member segments:
•
The API names of the data graphs must be:
- IndividualsCustomerEngmt for the data graph that's used to find advocates' segments that are
segmented on Individual.
- LoyaltyMembersCustomerEngmt for the data graph that's used to find advocates' segments that are
segmented on Loyalty Program Member.
•
The data graphs must follow this configuration:
- IndividualsCustomerEngmt
- Primary Data Model Object: Individual
- Related Data Model Objects: Individual > Loyalty Program Member > Loyalty Program Member
- Primary Key: Individual Id
- Key Qualifier: Key Qualifier Individual Id
- LoyaltyMembersCustomerEngmt
- Primary Data Model Object: Loyalty Program Member
- Related Data Model Object: Loyalty Program Member
- Primary Key: Id
- Key Qualifier: Key Qualifier Id
See Create a Data Graph.

Matching Rules and Duplicate Rules for Contacts and Person
Accounts
When you run a referral program, customers and their referred friends often try to sign up with the brand
more than one time. When a new customer signs up with the brand and joins a referral promotion, a
Contact record is created for the customer. Each time a referred friend signs up with the brand, a Contact
record and a Person Account record is created for the friend. Create duplicate rules and matching rules
to avoid creating duplicate contacts and person accounts for customers and their referred friends if they
try to sign up more than one time.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Duplicate Rule and Matching Rule Configuration
In the Referral Marketing org, create two matching rules for Contact and Person Account. In the criteria
for both matching rules, select Email as the field and Exact as the match method. After you create the
matching rules, create two duplicate rules for Contact and Person Account. Relate the duplicate rules to
their corresponding matching rules. The duplicate rules and their corresponding matching rules together
prevent customers and their friends from signing up with the brand multiple times by using the same
email address.
35

=== PAGE 40 ===
Referral Marketing Set Up Referral Marketing
You can also add actions and alert text that informs the person who is trying to sign up that they already
have a contact with the brand.
Tip If your brand wants to run additional checks before creating Contact and Person Account
records, you can add the checks in the matching rules and duplicate rules.
Matching Rule and Duplicate Rule Use
Here’s how Referral Marketing automatically uses the matching rules and the duplicate rules that you
create:
•
The Refer A Friend widget and the Advocate Enrollment Business API check whether a customer is
trying to sign up with the brand when they already have a contact.
•
The Referral Event Business API and the Referral Event action check whether:
- An advocate is trying to refer the same friend multiple times
- A referred friend with a Contact record and a Person Account record is trying to sign up with the
brand multiple times
See Also
Salesforce Help: Matching Rules
Salesforce Help: Duplicate Rules

WhatsApp Setup
To engage with customers via WhatsApp, you must set up your WhatsApp account in Marketing Cloud
Engagement. You need a customer's consent to receive messages from a business through WhatsApp.
This consent, called WhatsApp opt-in, is essential for businesses to initiate contact and build a list of
interested customers. The delivery of messages on WhatsApp depends on the sender's quality rating,
emphasizing the importance of maintaining high-quality communication.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
See Set Up Your WhatsApp Account in Marketing Cloud Engagement.
Considerations for Using WhatsApp
Marketing managers manage promotional WhatsApp messages to make communications more efficient
and personalized.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Here are a few things to keep in mind when you use WhatsApp.
•
Use Marketing Cloud Engagement to create templates for your transactional messages to use with
your active WhatsApp Business accounts.
•
Make sure that the message templates that you use are approved by WhatsApp Business Account
(WABA).
•
You must get opt-in consent from your intended recipients before you send a template message.
•
The header of the message template can contain text and images.
•
Depending on from where you attach your media files, different file formats and sizes are supported.
•
The Meta platform uses filters to ensure that messages adhere to their guidelines. Meta determines
whether your messages are delivered to customers.
38

•
If messages aren’t delivered to customers, use Chat Messaging Data Extract in Marketing Cloud
Engagement to find the reason for failure.
Marketing Cloud Engagement Business Unit Connection
Marketing Cloud Engagement journeys send emails to advocates and their friends at different stages of a
referral promotion. To send promotion emails with journeys, connect Referral Marketing with
Engagement business units. To set up the connection, complete the required setup tasks in your
Engagement business units and in Referral Marketing.
Watch the Business Unit Connection chapter of this video to understand how to connect a business unit
with Referral Marketing.
Watch the video: https://play.vidyard.com/TxSP9rw1hXiMxLpwMhc4xC
If you aren’t able to watch the video in full screen, open the video in a new tab: Prepare Your
Marketing Cloud Engagement Instance for Referral Marketing.
Reasons to Connect Referral Marketing with Multiple Business Units
Companies usually run multiple Marketing Cloud Engagement business units, and each business unit
contains the marketing assets for a specific brand, geography, or business line. Companies can also use a
similar strategy for their referral promotions. Companies can run a single referral program for accounting
purposes and create multiple referral promotions for different brands, geographies, or business lines.

How Business Units are Mapped to Promotions
Marketing managers can associate each referral promotion with a connected Engagement business unit.
When you activate a promotion, the promotion’s marketing journey and emails are automatically created
in the business unit associated with the promotion. Before marketing managers create promotions, they
work with the Referral Marketing admin to connect their promotion’s business unit with Referral
Marketing.
Benefits of Connecting Referral Marketing with Multiple Business Units
•
Marketing managers get access to the marketing journeys and emails of only the promotions that are
associated with the business unit that they have access to.
•
Marketing managers can customize the promotion journeys and emails as per the branding of their
39

business unit.
•
Executives can review and compare the performance and cost of referral promotions across different
business units.
•
Admins can select a unique send classification for each business unit.

Budget Management for Promotions and Campaigns in Referral
Marketing
Use Budget Management to allocate funds, estimate utilization, and track spending for promotions and
campaigns. Define hierarchical structures to organize budgets based on business requirements, and
track utilization across time periods for financial control and accounting.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Required Editions
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Strategic Budget Allocation and Management
•
Structure budgets hierarchically based on geographies, lines of business (LOB), organizational units, or
business units. This hierarchical model supports clear ownership, rollup visibility, and governance
across the organization.
•
Define budgets for specific fiscal periods to track the utilization precisely over time and to get granular
financial control.
•
Marketing managers raise requests against the available overall budget. After approval, allocate the
funds to promotions or campaigns activities, and track and monitor expenses incurred during
execution. This approval process makes sure that your promotion and campaign spending aligns with
the approved financial limits.
50

Use Case Examples
•
Establish budgets for different geographies, such as Asia-Pacific (APAC) and Europe, the Middle East,
and Africa (EMEA). Track budgets for each region's campaign under it.
•
Define high-level campaign budgets, and then group the related promotion budgets under them as
child records.
•
Create budgets for each promotion-related activity such as Social media ads, awareness programs,
and training. Then, group these budgets to define the overall promotion budget.

=== PAGE 57 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
How Referral Programs and Promotions Work Together
Different dynamics come into play when a brand decides to run a referral program. The timing and the
messaging for the brand’s referral program can vary depending on the target audience and the timing of
the planned customer outreach programs. Referral Marketing is designed to support the unique needs of
each customer.
A referral program can consist of multiple promotions. Each promotion can be tailored to the referral
program's various needs. Brands can run evergreen and time-bound referral promotions that are targeted
towards different sections of the brand's customer base or all customers.
Example Cloud Kicks wants to run one evergreen promotion that runs throughout the year and
offers a US$10 discount for the advocates and their referred friends. They also want to run two time-
bound promotions, one during the company’s anniversary week and another on December 31 and
January 1. The marketing manager creates one referral program and adds three promotions to it.
The evergreen promotion has a start date but no end date. The company anniversary promotion
runs for a week and the year-end promotion’s start date is December 31 and the end date is January
1.
Example Cloud Kicks wants to run a referral program for their advocates in France and Canada. For
France, they want to reward the advocates and their referred friends with a 10% discount voucher.
For Canada, Cloud Kicks wants to provide a 15% discount to the advocates and a 10% voucher to
the advocates’ friends. In this case, Cloud Kicks can run two promotions, one for each country.
Example Cloud Kicks wants to run a referral program that consists of an evergreen promotion for all
its customers and a time-bound promotion for a specific customer group. For the evergreen
promotion, the marketing manager selects a start date but doesn't select an end date or a target
audience. For the time-bound promotion, the marketing manager selects a start date, an end date,
and a Data 360 segment campaign that consists of the promotion's target audience.
Explore and Learn
Watch this video to understand how to create a referral program and design its promotions.
Watch the video: https://play.vidyard.com/vzDMwuh97rQSay25RAojMp
If you can’t watch the video in full screen, open the video on a new tab: Design a Referral Program.
11.. Create a Referral Program
The launchpad for any referral strategy is the referral program. After marketing managers create a
referral program, they can manage and implement all aspects for their referral strategy from the
referral program.
22.. Add Rewards
Referral programs incentivize the advocates and referred friends for engaging with the brand.
Marketing managers can design a range of rewards such as commission payouts, cashbacks, or gift
cards that appeal to the target audience. They can add multiple rewards types in a referral program
53

=== PAGE 58 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
and offer different rewards to advocates and their friends. If a referral program includes multiple
promotions, each promotion can offer a unique set of rewards to both advocates and their friends.
33.. Add Advocates
Advocates of a referral program are the customers who are willing to refer your brand to their friends.
Marketing managers can either add all customers as advocates or add a select set of customers to the
referral program. If the number of customers to be added is small, marketing managers can add the
advocates one by one. Or, marketing managers can work with the admin to set up a process that adds
all the advocates simultaneously.
44.. Promotion Template
Promotion templates determine the configuration of promotions. In a promotion template, decide
stage names, the stages at which advocates and their referred friends are rewarded, and the activities
that rewards are provided for. Each promotion is based on a promotion template. The promotion
template decides the promotion's stage names, the activities for which the promotion rewards
advocates and their referred friends, and the promotion's email content. Before you create a
promotion, decide if you want to use an existing promotion template or create a unique template for
your promotion.
55.. Create a Promotion
Promotions are the primary vehicle that runs your referral program. Marketing managers can design
different types of promotions with varying duration, audience, rewards, and stages.
66.. Use Marketing Cloud Next for Outbound Engagement
When you set your communication method as Marketing Cloud, you must add Marketing Cloud Next
as an outbound engagement to send emails at different stages of the promotion journey. Emails at the
Promotion Launched stage are segment-based and uses Data 360 segments to target the right
audience. For all other stages, emails are event-based, that trigger a flow for content distribution.

Here are a few other key fields to consider while you create voucher definitions:
•
Effective Date—Select the date from when the voucher definition can be used to issue vouchers.
•
Cost Per Voucher—Enter the liability that the company incurs each time a voucher is issued using the
definition.
•
Partial Redeemable—Select to let advocates and friends use the voucher across multiple purchases.
This option is available only for fixed value vouchers.
•
Code Prefix, Code Suffix, and Autogenerated Code Length—Enter the prefix, suffix, and length of the
voucher code.
The prefix and the suffix are used in the unique automatically generated voucher code, and the length
determines the voucher code length. If you don’t specify any of these values, a unique eight-character
code is generated for each issued voucher. Advocates and friends use their voucher code to redeem
their voucher.

Add Advocates
Advocates of a referral program are the customers who are willing to refer your brand to their friends.
Marketing managers can either add all customers as advocates or add a select set of customers to the
referral program. If the number of customers to be added is small, marketing managers can add the
advocates one by one. Or, marketing managers can work with the admin to set up a process that adds all
the advocates simultaneously.

Promotion Template
Promotion templates determine the configuration of promotions. In a promotion template, decide stage
names, the stages at which advocates and their referred friends are rewarded, and the activities that
rewards are provided for. Each promotion is based on a promotion template. The promotion template
decides the promotion's stage names, the activities for which the promotion rewards advocates and their
referred friends, and the promotion's email content. Before you create a promotion, decide if you want
to use an existing promotion template or create a unique template for your promotion.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Default Promotion Template
Referral Marketing provides a promotion template by default: Refer a Friend. This template isn't available
for marketing managers to view or customize. Here's how the Refer a Friend promotion template is
configured:
Stage Name What Happens At This Stage
Promotion Launched Advocates are invited to join the promotion.
Advocate Joins Promotion Advocates join the promotion.
Advocate Refers Friend Advocates refer their friends.
Friend Signs Up Referred friends sign up and are rewarded for
signing up.
Friend Completes First Purchase Friends complete their first purchase and the
advocate who referred the friends is rewarded.
Promotions that use the Refer a Friend template reward both advocates and their referred friends.
Friends are rewarded when they sign up and advocates are rewarded when their referred friends
complete their first purchase.
Custom Promotion Templates
From the Promotion Templates related list on a referral program, you can view the promotion templates
that team members have already created. If none of the promotion templates work for your promotion,
you can go ahead and create a promotion template. After you create a promotion template, other
marketing managers and you can reuse the template to create similar promotions.
63

=== PAGE 68 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Here are a few advantages of creating a promotion template.
•
Change the stage names as per the needs of your promotion.
•
Choose whether you want to reward both advocates and their friends, either, or none of them.
•
Select the activity that advocates and their referred friends get rewards for.
•
Add extended rewards for advocates and referrals.
You can reward both advocates and their referred friends at the same stage but can't reward them for
the same activity. Also, you can reward advocates and their friends only one time each in the promotion's
journey.

Here's how the last three stages are designed in most referral promotions:
•
Third stage—Advocates refer their friends.
•
Fourth stage—Referred friends engage with the brand for the first time.
Based on your brand and your industry's requirements, the way in which referred friends engage with
your brand can differ. In the financial services industry, referred friends engage with the brand for the
first time when they open a bank account. In travel and hospitality, referred friends engage with the
brand for the first time when they book a stay.
•
Fifth stage—Referred friends complete an activity that closes the promotion's journey.
In the financial services industry, the journey can close when the referred friends complete their first
bank account transaction. In travel and hospitality, the journey can close when the referred friends
check out after their first stay.
Tip Name the stages in line with the activity that you want the advocates or their friends to
complete during the stage. For example, name the stage Friend Opens Bank Account if you want
friends to open a bank account on the fourth stage.

=== PAGE 74 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Create a Promotion
Promotions are the primary vehicle that runs your referral program. Marketing managers can design
different types of promotions with varying duration, audience, rewards, and stages.
Referral Promotion Prerequisites
Before marketing managers design a referral promotion, they must ensure that all the information
that's required to design a promotion is already available.
Design a Referral Promotion Using a Guided Flow
Use a guided flow to design and launch a referral promotion within minutes. The guided flow consists
of four simple steps that let marketing managers add the promotion’s rewards, decide the target
audience, set limits, and design the promotion’s marketing content.
70

=== PAGE 75 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Activate Promotions
Activate your promotion on the day when you want to launch the promotion for the target audience. If
you've activated the promotion's launch email, then the launch email is sent to the target audience
after the promotion is activated. After the promotion is activated, advocates can start joining the
promotion from the promotion's start date.
What Happens After a Promotion is Activated
After a promotion is activated, journeys are created for each stage of the promotion in the Marketing
Cloud Engagement business unit associated with the promotion. Advocates who belong to the
promotion's referral program and belong to the promotion's target audience can join the promotion
and refer their friends from the promotion's start date. Referred friends can also start to engage with
the brand for the first time by using the advocate's referral link or code.
Promotion FAQs
Review the frequently asked questions about referral promotions and understand how you can work
around some of the limitations.
Customize Promotion Journeys in Marketing Cloud Engagement
The journeys that are created in Referral Marketing’s connected Marketing Cloud Engagement org for
activated promotions can be customized after a promotion is activated. The journeys can be
customized based on the promotion’s marketing and communications strategy. For example, you can
add a push notification to the journeys.
Referral Promotion Prerequisites
Before marketing managers design a referral promotion, they must ensure that all the information that's
required to design a promotion is already available.
Explore and Learn
Watch this video to learn the key aspects of a referral promotion and how marketing managers can plan
for their promotions in Salesforce Referral Marketing.
Watch the video: https://play.vidyard.com/7sp7hLWjyS4Wr3UPji3kZ4
If you can’t watch the video in full screen, open the video on a new tab: Plan Your Promotion’s
Design.
Referral Promotion Strategy
Each brand has a unique way of designing and marketing its referral program. Referral Marketing helps
a brand design and run multiple promotions simultaneously or one promotion at a time based on the
brand’s marketing strategy. The brand can also tailor each promotion’s stages, rewards, audience, and
outreach strategy based on its business needs.
Promotion Audience
B2C referral promotions can be targeted either towards your entire customer base or towards specific
customer groups. Before you use the B2C Referral Promotion guided flow to design a promotion,
decide the promotion’s target audience. If you want to target a specific customer group, you can filter
71

A promotion rewards advocates and their referred friends when an eligible activity is completed.
Before you create a referral promotion, decide the promotion's eligible activities for advocates and
their referred friends. Eligible activities are represented as journal subtypes in Salesforce.
Promotion Rewards
Based on the promotion template that you want to use for your promotion, decide the rewards that
you want to offer as part of the promotion. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and
their friends, then decide whether you want to give the same reward to advocates and their friends, or
different rewards.

Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Promotion Audience
B2C referral promotions can be targeted either towards your entire customer base or towards specific
customer groups. Before you use the B2C Referral Promotion guided flow to design a promotion, decide
the promotion’s target audience. If you want to target a specific customer group, you can filter the target
audience by using a Data 360 segment or a campaign.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Find Out The Customers Who Are Most Likely to Refer Their Friends
Before you filter your audience, use the Customer Likelihood to Referring dashboard to find out the
customers who are most likely to refer their friends. The dashboard scores customers on their probability
to refer and provides demographic insights on the probability to refer.
Segment Target Audience by Using Data 360 Segment
You can segment on contacts in your org in Data 360. With Data 360, you can segment the contacts by
using the data available in your org and by using the data from external sources. If your company uses
Marketing Cloud Next as the promotion communication method, you must select Data 360 segments as
the target audience for promotions.
Before you create a promotion that’s targeted towards a segment, ensure that the segment’s status is
Active.
To learn how to create Data 360 segments, see Segmentation.
Segment Target Audience by Using Campaign
You can also filter your promotion’s target audience by using campaigns. In a campaign, add the contacts
who you want to include as the promotion’s target audience.
To learn how to create campaigns and add contacts as campaign members, see Working with
Campaigns and Manage Campaign Members.
Important To create a campaign to filter contacts, ask your admin to select the Marketing User
permission in your User record.
74

=== PAGE 79 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
What Happens if the Target Audience is Filtered Outside Salesforce
You can create a campaign and then work with your admin to:
•
Map the filtered target audience to the contacts in the org
•
Add the filtered contacts as members by using reports or the Data Import Wizard
What Happens After Segments or Campaigns are Created
After you create segments or campaigns, you can select a segment or campaign members as a
promotion’s target audience in the Rewards and Limits step of the Referral Promotion Guided Setup.
Eligible Activities for Promotions
A promotion rewards advocates and their referred friends when an eligible activity is completed. Before
you create a referral promotion, decide the promotion's eligible activities for advocates and their referred
friends. Eligible activities are represented as journal subtypes in Salesforce.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Journal Type and Journal Subtype Usage
•
Journal type—Used to identify activities that belong to advocates and their referred friends.
•
Journal subtype—Used to uniquely identify the type of activity completed by advocates and their
friends.
Default Journal Type and Journal Subtype
Referral Marketing comes with one journal type: Referral. There’s also a set of journal subtypes associated
with the Referral journal type by default.
•
Advocate Enrollment—Used to identity an activity where an advocate has joined a promotion.
You can't reward advocates for joining a promotion.
•
Referral Sign Up—Used to identify an activity where a referred friend signs up with the brand.
•
Referral Purchase—Used to identify an activity where a referred friend completes a purchase after
signing up with the brand.
•
Advocate Purchase—Used to identify an activity where an advocate completes a purchase.
•
Advocate Reward—Used to identify the activity where the referral promotion rewards the advocate.
Tip To view the journal types and subtypes that are available in your org, you can access the list
75

=== PAGE 80 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
views from the App Launcher.
Eligible Activities of Your Promotion
Apart from the Advocate Enrollment journal subtype, you can use any of the other journal subtypes to
identify the activities for which you want to reward advocates and their referred friends.
The journal subtypes that are provided by default don't always relate to the activities that you want to
qualify for rewards. You can create journal subtypes and name them based on the activities you want to
qualify for rewards. The journal subtypes that you create must be associated with the Referral journal
type.
Example The marketing manager of a bank wants to reward referred friends for opening an account
and wants to reward advocates when their friends complete their first credit card transaction. For
these two eligible activities, the marketing manager creates two journal subtypes: Referred Friend
Opened Bank Account and Referred Friend Completed First Bank Transaction.
Example The marketing manager at a retail brand wants to reward advocates when their referred
friends sign up, and reward friends after they complete a purchase of US$75 or above. For the
advocate's eligible activity, the marketing manager decides to reuse the Referral Sign Up journal
type. For the friend's eligible activity, the marketing manager creates a journal subtype named
Friend's Order Value is $75.
Tip Often brands tend to run multiple referral promotions where advocates and their friends are
rewarded for the same activity across promotions. Marketing teams can create a set of journal
subtypes that represent all the activities for which the brand's referral promotions can offer rewards
and reuse the journal subtypes across similar promotions.
Promotion Rewards
Based on the promotion template that you want to use for your promotion, decide the rewards that you
want to offer as part of the promotion. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and their
friends, then decide whether you want to give the same reward to advocates and their friends, or
different rewards.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
After you finalize the promotion's rewards, review the referral program's existing voucher definitions and
extended reward definitions to check whether any of them match your promotion's requirements. If
none of the definitions match your promotion's requirements, create voucher definitions and extended
reward definitions unique to your promotion.

Design a Referral Promotion Using a Guided Flow
Use a guided flow to design and launch a referral promotion within minutes. The guided flow consists of
four simple steps that let marketing managers add the promotion’s rewards, decide the target audience,
set limits, and design the promotion’s marketing content.
11.. Promotion Definition
In the first step of the guided flow, define the key attributes of the promotion.
22.. Rewards and Audience
In the second step of the guided flow, select the promotion’s rewards, limits, and target audience.
33.. Communication Assets
On the third step in the guided flow, customize and enable the promotion’s communication channels
and the Refer A Friend widget. The communication channels include email and WhatsApp.
44.. Summary
In the last step of the guided flow, review the journey of the advocates and their referred friends in the
promotion.

Promotion Definition
In the first step of the guided flow, define the key attributes of the promotion.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Key Promotion Attributes
Define these key attributes of the promotion:
Attribute Function
Name The name of the referral promotion that’s used in your customer-
facing communication.
Description
Your brand’s internal goals or objectives for the referral promotion.
Description is an optional attribute.
Promotion duration
The start and end dates of the promotion determine how long the
promotion runs. During the duration of the promotion:
•
Advocates can join the referral program and refer their friends
•
Friends can sign up and make their first purchase
•
Advocates and friends can be rewarded
If you’re creating an evergreen promotion, don’t specify an end
date.
Promotion code
An advocate’s referral code consists of the promotion code and the
advocate’s unique code.
Friends use their advocate’s referral code to sign up. The code is also
used to uniquely identify the promotion that the referral activities of
advocates and their referred friends belong to. Since the referral
code consists of the promotion, it’s easy to identify how promotions
are performing.
After you enter a promotion code and move to the next step of the
guided flow, you can't change the code.
Promotion page URL The URL is used to create the unique referral links for the advocates
79

=== PAGE 84 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Attribute Function
who join the promotion. The URL that you specify is suffixed with
the advocate’s unique referral code. An advocate can view and
share their referral link from the Refer A Friend widget after they join
the promotion.
Referral promotion template
The promotion template that you want to base your promotion on.
The promotion's template decides whom the promotion rewards,
the stage at which the rewards are provided, and the emails that are
available for the promotion and the email content.
You can use an active template to build your promotion. After you
select a template and move to the next step of the guided flow, you
can't change the promotion's template.
Business unit
The Marketing Cloud Engagement business unit where the
promotion’s marketing journeys and emails are created when the
promotion is activated.
If the admin connects Referral Marketing with only one
Engagement business unit, it’s automatically selected.
If you can’t find the business unit that you want to associate with
the promotion, ask your admin to connect the business unit with
Referral Marketing. After the admin sets up the connection, you can
associate a connected business unit with your promotion.
See Also
Salesforce Help: Promotion's Template
Rewards and Audience
In the second step of the guided flow, select the promotion’s rewards, limits, and target audience.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Rewards
The promotion template that you select for a promotion decides who the promotion's rewards and at
which stage the rewards are provided. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and their
80

=== PAGE 85 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
referred friends, then you can select the reward definitions you want to use to offer the rewards. You can
offer the same reward or different rewards to advocates and their referred friends.
If the promotion's template rewards either advocates or their referred friends, then you can only select a
reward for the person who the promotion template rewards. If the promotion's template doesn't reward
anyone, you can't select a reward in the Referral Promotion guided flow.
Selct rewards for advocates and friends for the referral stages.
Reward Type description
Voucher The defined vouchers appear in the Reward picklist. Select a
voucher.
Extended Rewards The defined extended rewards are listed in the Reward Type picklist.
Select a reward and enter a reward name and a value.
Based on the rewards you select, the communication assets display voucher or extended reward details.
Tip Before you create a promotion, add the voucher definitions and extended reward definitions on
the referral program page for the rewards that you want to offer advocates and their referred
friends.
Limits
To stay within the budget of the referral promotion and to ensure that they aren’t fraudulent referrals,
you can set limits for advocates. If a promotion template doesn't reward advocates, then you can add
limits for advocates of promotions that use the template.
Limit Type Purpose
Reward limit
Limit for the number of times an advocate can be rewarded for
successful referrals. The limit can be set for a fixed duration:
•
Promotion duration—The limit is applicable for the complete
duration of the promotion. After an advocate reaches the limit,
they’re no longer rewarded for any successful referral.
•
Calendar year—The limit is applicable for a calendar year. After an
advocate reaches the limit, they aren’t rewarded for any
successful referrals during the current year. They’re again
rewarded for the successful referrals in the next year.
For example, if the promotion’s reward limit is 5 and the advocate
was already rewarded five times in 2024, they aren’t rewarded
when their sixth referral signs up in 2024. But if the referral signs
up in 2025, the advocate is rewarded.
81

=== PAGE 86 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Limit Type Purpose
Daily referral limit
Limit the number of referrals that advocates can submit in a day.
The limit is only applicable for the referral emails that advocates
send from the Refer A Friend widget. The advocate can share their
referral link or code with their friends by using other channels such
as their personal email account and social media as many times as
they want.
Target Audience
You can decide the target audience of each promotion. Only program advocates who are part of the
promotion’s target audience can join the promotion and refer their friends.
You can select the target audience from these options.
Target Audience Type Purpose
All advocates All the advocates of the referral program are the
promotion’s target audience.
Campaign members
Advocates who are members of the selected
campaign are the promotion’s target audience.
To ensure that an advocate is part of the
campaign, the advocate’s contact record must be
a member of the campaign.
Data 360 segment members
Advocates who are part of the selected Data 360
segment are the promotion’s target audience.
To select a Data 360 segment, the org must have
Data 360 enabled.
If your company uses Marketing Cloud Next as the promotion communication method, you must use
select Data 360 segments as the target audience for promotions.
Tip Before you select the promotion’s target audience, use the Customer Likelihood to Referring
dashboard to find out the customers who are most likely to refer their friends. The dashboard scores
customers on their probability to refer and provides demographic insights about the probability to
refer.
82

Emails and WhatsApp Messages
Referral Marketing includes a set of email and WhatsApp message templates. The promotion template
that you select for a promotion determines the electronic messages that are available for the
promotion. The content of the electronic messages changes based on when the selected promotion
template rewards advocates and their referred friends.
The Refer a Friend Widget
Every referral promotion comes with a widget that allows advocates to sign up for the promotion and
send referral emails to their friends. The widget also allows people visiting the brand’s site to sign up
with the brand and then join the referral promotion. After you customize the widget based on the
brand’s guideline, admins can embed the widget’s flexcard on Experience Cloud sites or external sites.
On the Referral Promotion guided flow, the widget is placed in the Promotion Launched stage.
Emails and WhatsApp Messages
Referral Marketing includes a set of email and WhatsApp message templates. The promotion template
that you select for a promotion determines the electronic messages that are available for the promotion.
The content of the electronic messages changes based on when the selected promotion template
rewards advocates and their referred friends.

Stage 3
The third stage in a promotion is known as Advocate Refers Friend but the name of the stage can be

advocates refer their friends can differ based on your business requirements or your industry. In the
financial services industry, advocates can invite their friends to open a bank account. In travel and
hospitality, advocates invite their friends to book a stay with the hotel.

Message Sender
A Marketing Cloud Engagement sender profile sends messages using email and WhatsApp to advocates
and their referred friends. Before you create promotions, admins set up a connection between Referral
Marketing and Engagement business units. For each connection, the admin selects a send classification.
The sender profile of the send classification that's selected for the promotion's Engagement business unit
sends the promotion's messages.
Sometimes admins don't connect Referral Marketing with an Engagement business unit when they’re
testing the capabilities of Referral Marketing in a sandbox or a non-production org. When a business unit
isn't connected with Referral Marketing, organization-wide email addresses send the promotion's emails.
In this scenario, you can select which organization-wide email address sends each email.

The Refer a Friend Widget
Every referral promotion comes with a widget that allows advocates to sign up for the promotion and
send referral emails to their friends. The widget also allows people visiting the brand’s site to sign up with
the brand and then join the referral promotion. After you customize the widget based on the brand’s
guideline, admins can embed the widget’s flexcard on Experience Cloud sites or external sites. On the
Referral Promotion guided flow, the widget is placed in the Promotion Launched stage.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Widget States
The Refer A Friend widget consists of these states:
State What Viewers Can Do
New Advocate Sign up as a new customer and then join the promotion.
Advocate Not Registered Join the referral promotion.
Registered Advocate Share their referral code with friends via email or Social media.
Display Error If this error occurs multiple times, admins can verify the
configurations used to embed the widget on the site.
Important If your brand is running the referral program in a geographic region where the brand
must get the consent of advocates before they join or refer their friends, you can edit the widget’s
flexcard in Omnistudio’s Flexcard Designer to add a link to the referral promotion’s terms and
conditions and add a checkbox for advocates to provide their consent.
Widget State Support
The capabilities supported by the widget depend on where you host the widget.
•
Experience Cloud sites: Only authenticated users can access the widget. The widget state shown to the
logged user depends on whether they signed up for the promotion.
Important Guest user access to the widget from Experience Cloud sites isn’t supported.
•
External sites: The state of the widget depends on the authentication and authorization information
passed by using OmniOut. Use proxy servers or any other mechanisms to manage this information.
Here’s a table that describes who can view each widget state.

that Referral Marketing uses the class when users access the widget.

Sample Apex Class to Create a Refer a Friend Widget
A sample Apex class that you can customize to create a custom widget that meets your business
requirements.
global with sharing class WidgetReferAFriend implements System.Callable {
Map<String, String> messages = new Map<String, String>();
global Object call(String action, Map<String, Object> arguments) {
Map<String, Object> input = (Map<String, Object>)arguments.get('inpu
t');
Map<String, Object> output = (Map<String, Object>)arguments.get('outpu
t');
Map<String, Object> options = (Map<String, Object>)arguments.get('opti
ons');
initMessages(output);
if (action == 'load') {
return load(input, output, options);
}
if (action == 'enrollNew') {
return enrollNew(input, output, options);
}
if (action == 'enrollExisting') {
return enrollExisting(input, output, options);
}

return null;

ails because the specified email ID and contact ID don’t belong to the same Co
ntact record. Specify the email ID and the ID of the same Contact record and t
ry again.');

u specified the details of a Contact record that isn’t available in the org. S
pecify the details of a valid Contact record and try again.');

tact record isn’t associated with the person viewing the widget. Try again aft
er you associate a Contact record with the user viewing the widget.');

private Map<String, Object> load(Map<String, Object> input, Map<String, Ob
ject> output, Map<String, Object> options) {
Long startTimeInMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
String contactId = (String)input.get('contactId');
String promotionCode = (String)input.get('promotionCode');
String programName = (String)input.get('programName');

private Map<String, Object> validatePromotionDate(Map<String, Object> prom
otionDetails) {
Map<String, Object> details = new Map<String, Object>();
details.put('status', 'valid');
Date startDate = Date.valueOf((String)promotionDetails.get('startDat
e'));
Date endDate = null;
if (promotionDetails.get('endDate') != null) {
endDate = Date.valueOf((String)promotionDetails.get('endDate'));
}
if (startDate > Date.today()) {
details.put('errorMessage', messages.get('PromotionNotStarted'));
details.put('status', 'invalid');
} else if (endDate != null && endDate < Date.today()) {
details.put('errorMessage', messages.get('PromotionExpired'));
details.put('status', 'invalid');
}
return details;
}

private String generateRandomString(Integer len) {
final String chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789';
String randStr = '';
while (randStr.length() < len) {
Integer idx = Math.mod(Math.abs(Crypto.getRandomInteger()), char
s.length());
randStr += chars.substring(idx, idx+1);
}
return randStr;
}

private void processTransactionJournal(String transactionJournalId, String
programName) {
Invocable.Action action = Invocable.Action.createStandardAction('runPr
ogramProcessForTransactionJournal');
action.setInvocationParameter('transactionJournalId', transactionJourn
alId);
List<Invocable.Action.Result> results = action.invoke();
for (Invocable.Action.Result result : results) {
if (result.isSuccess()) {
System.debug('Success: Transaction Journal processed successfull
y.');
} else {
System.debug('Error: ' + result.getErrors()[0].getMessage());
}
}
}

Callout What You Can Review
1 Verify your promotion's duration, target audience, and rewards. If
something isn't right, you can go back and make the required
changes.
2 Verify whether you’ve activated the emails that you want to send
during the promotion's journey. Inactive emails aren't sent to
advocates and their referred friends. If the promotion's strategy is to
enable advocates to join the promotion and refer their friends from
an external site or an Experience Cloud site, ensure that the widget
is active.
Activate Promotions
Activate your promotion on the day when you want to launch the promotion for the target audience. If
you've activated the promotion's launch email, then the launch email is sent to the target audience after
the promotion is activated. After the promotion is activated, advocates can start joining the promotion
from the promotion's start date.

It takes a few minutes for the promotion to be activated. You can review the activation status in the
Journey tab of the promotion.
After activation, journeys are created in the promotion's Marketing Cloud Engagement business unit for
each promotion stage that contains active emails. The journeys automatically send emails to advocates
and their referrals as they progress through each promotion stage.
If your communication method is Marketing Cloud Next, you can update the promotion journey stages.
What Happens After a Promotion is Activated
After a promotion is activated, journeys are created for each stage of the promotion in the Marketing
Cloud Engagement business unit associated with the promotion. Advocates who belong to the
promotion's referral program and belong to the promotion's target audience can join the promotion and
refer their friends from the promotion's start date. Referred friends can also start to engage with the
brand for the first time by using the advocate's referral link or code.

=== PAGE 117 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Marketing Cloud Engagement
Marketing Cloud Engagement Journeys
Referral Marketing uses journeys in Marketing Cloud Engagement to send messages to advocates and
their referred friends as they progress along the promotion stages. A promotion's journeys are created
in the Engagement business unit that's associated with the promotion.
Marketing Cloud Next
When you activate a promotion, campaigns and flows work together to distribute content. Each
campaign you create comes with a preconfigured flow to get you started. A flow executes the
campaign and automates content distribution. You can set an event in the flow that automatically
sends the communication when the event is triggered.
Salesforce Email Or External Email Services
When you activate the promotion, Salesforce Email or the external email services use a flow builder or
Apex based logic to leverage the business APIs, invocable actions or process rules to distribute
content.
Marketing Cloud Engagement Journeys
Referral Marketing uses journeys in Marketing Cloud Engagement to send messages to advocates and
their referred friends as they progress along the promotion stages. A promotion's journeys are created in
the Engagement business unit that's associated with the promotion.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Marketing Cloud Engagement
Important Journeys are automatically created for promotions associated with an Engagement
business unit that's connected with Referral Marketing.
Journey Configuration
Unique journeys are created for each stage of a promotion. If a stage sends messages to both advocates
and their referred friends, two journeys are created for the stage. One journey sends messages to
advocates and another sends messages to the referred friends. Only active messages of a promotion
stage are added to its journey. A journey isn't created if a stage doesn't have active messages.
The names of journeys consist of three parts. The first part contains the name of the stage that the
journey belongs to. The second part indicates who the journey sends messages to, advocates or their
referred friends. The last part of the journey name contains the promotion code. The naming convention
of journeys enables marketing managers to easily locate journeys in Journey Builder.
When rewarding advocates and referred friends, journeys are executed immediately after a voucher is
113

=== PAGE 118 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
issued. However, for promotions offering extended rewards, journey execution is triggered only after the
reward value is finalized. This ensures that Marketing Cloud Engagement emails automatically reflect any
updated or dynamically calculated reward amounts. See Orchestration of Extended Rewards.
Along with each journey, a data extension is also created. A journey's data extension determines who the
journey sends messages to. The data extension's name consists of the stage that the extension belongs
to and the code of the promotion that it belongs to.
Stage 1—Promotion Launched
For the first stage of a promotion, only one journey is created because the messages of the first stage are
sent only to advocates. The journey sends the promotion launch message six hours after the promotion
is activated. The message is sent to all advocates who are part of the promotion's referral program and
are part of the promotion's target audience. If an advocate is added to the referral program after the
promotion is activated, the journey sends the promotion launch message to new advocates after they're
added. After the journey's first run, journey is scheduled to run every hour.
After the launch message is sent, the journey also sends the reminder message to advocates who didn't
join the promotion.
The journey uses the PromotionLaunched data extension to get the details of whom to send the
messages to and resolve the message merge fields.
Tip To change the delivery schedule of messages, see Automation Studio.
Stage 2—Advocate Joins Promotion
For the second stage of a promotion, only one journey is created because the messages of the second
stage are sent only to advocates. The journey sends a message with a unique referral URL to advocates
who have joined the promotion. If an advocate doesn't refer any of their friends, the journey sends the
reminder message.
The journey uses the AdvocateJoinsPromotion data extension to get the details of whom to send the
messages to and resolve the message merge fields. The journey is designed to run whenever an advocate
is added to the data extension.
Stage 3
In the third stage of a promotion, messages are sent to the referred friends. If the promotion's template
rewards advocates during the third stage, a message is also sent to the advocates to inform them about
the referral reward.
Here are the journeys that are created for the third stage:

When you activate a promotion, campaigns and flows work together to distribute content. Each

and automates content distribution. You can set an event in the flow that automatically sends the
communication when the event is triggered.

Promotion FAQs
Review the frequently asked questions about referral promotions and understand how you can work
around some of the limitations.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Can I Update the Content or HTML of Promotion Emails?
Yes, the emails that you customize and activate for your promotions are stored in the Referral Marketing
org as email templates. You can update the content or the HTML of the promotion emails based on your
brand’s requirements. Before you update the activated emails of a promotion, ensure that the promotion
isn’t activated. After you update the emails, activate the promotion. This ensures that the journeys and
email templates that are created in the connected Marketing Cloud Engagement business unit
associated with the promotion contain your changes.
Tip To customize an email after you design the promotion and activate the emails that you require
for it, go to the Promotion Stage Email template list view. Open the email template of the
promotion email that you want to update. You can update the email content from the Message
Content section. To update the HTML of the email, switch to the source view in HTML Value.To help
you identify the email template for a promotion email, the email template name consists of the
name of the promotion stage that the email template belongs to and the promotion’s code.
Can Promotion Emails be Sent Without a Connected Engagement Business
Unit?
We recommend that you connect Referral Marketing with at least one Engagement business unit and
send promotion emails in a journey.
Reminder emails aren’t available for you to customize and use in your referral promotion communication
if Referral Marketing isn’t connected to Engagement.
Can I Select a Campaign That Consists of Leads as a Promotion’s Target
Audience?
No, the target audience of a promotion is always advocates who have a Contact record in the org. If you
select a campaign to filter a promotion’s target audience, the campaign members must be contacts.
119

=== PAGE 124 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
What Happens if the Org Reaches the Promotion Template Limit?
Email templates are automatically created for all stages of a promotion when a promotion is activated.
The email templates are used to send emails to advocates and their referred friends. To stay within the
email template limit, delete the email templates that belong to the promotions that are past their end
date or were created for testing purposes. Trial and free orgs can store up to 500 email templates. To
increase the email template limit for your org, contact Salesforce Customer Support.
Are Emails, Journeys, and Data Extensions Automatically Deleted When I
Delete a Promotion?
No, you must manually delete emails, journeys, and data extensions that are created for promotions
after you delete the promotion. If you deactivate a promotion, its journeys automatically stop running in
Engagement.
See Also
Salesforce Help: Email Templates in Lightning Experience
Salesforce Help: Journeys and Messages
Customize Promotion Journeys in Marketing Cloud Engagement
The journeys that are created in Referral Marketing’s connected Marketing Cloud Engagement org for
activated promotions can be customized after a promotion is activated. The journeys can be customized
based on the promotion’s marketing and communications strategy. For example, you can add a push
notification to the journeys.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
How Can You Customize Journeys
If you want to customize a journey, first find the journey on the Journeys Dashboard in the Engagement
business unit associated with the promotion. Each journey name consists of the name of the promotion
stage that it represents and is suffixed with the code of the promotion that it belongs to.
After you open the journey, create another version of the journey. Customize the new version based on
your requirements and activate the version. Also, ensure that the version that was automatically created
is paused.
If a promotion is deactivated and updated in the Referral Marketing org, and then activated again,
another version is created for each journey of the promotion. The new journey versions don’t contain
120

=== PAGE 125 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
your customization. In this case, create another version and copy the customizations from the version
where you previously added your changes and add them to the version that you created. Again, ensure
that you activate the version that you want to run and pause the versions that you don’t want to run.
How Can You Customize Emails
Promotion journeys consist of the emails that were activated for the promotion. The emails are saved as
email templates in the business unit associated with the promotion and can be accessed from Content
Builder in Engagement. Each email template is named the same as its name on the promotion’s guided
flow and is suffixed with the code of the promotion that it belongs to.
You can open the email template and customize them based on your requirements. And the changes are
automatically populated in the active version of the journey that the email template is used in.
If a promotion is deactivated and its emails are updated in the Referral Marketing org, and then the
promotion is activated again, the Engagement email templates are updated with the changes. And the
changes that you made in Engagement are lost. If you customize the email templates in Engagement,
make sure that you copy over those changes when editing the email template in the Referral Marketing
org.
What are the Considerations for Customization
If you customize the journeys and email templates in Engagement, the customizations don’t sync back to
the related referral promotion’s configuration and to the related email templates in the Referral
Marketing org.
You must not customize these things in journeys and email templates:
•
Names of the journeys and email templates
•
Entry event configuration of the journeys and the associated data extensions
See Also
Salesforce Help: Email Templates in Lightning Experience
Salesforce Help: Create Emails in Content Builder
Use Marketing Cloud Next for Outbound Engagement
When you set your communication method as Marketing Cloud, you must add Marketing Cloud Next as
an outbound engagement to send emails at different stages of the promotion journey. Emails at the
Promotion Launched stage are segment-based and uses Data 360 segments to target the right audience.
For all other stages, emails are event-based, that trigger a flow for content distribution.
