Configure Referral Processes
After marketing managers create the referral program and add its promotions, the admin or the
developer can configure the everyday processes. The processes include advocate enrollment, activity
tracking, and voucher redemption.
Advocate Enrollment
After marketing managers activate referral promotions, the marketing manager, the admin, and the
developer can decide how they want the brand’s advocates to join the referral promotions. For a
promotion, the brand can choose to either embed the promotion’s widget on a site or use a business
API to process advocate enrollments.
122

=== PAGE 127 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
Referral Activity Tracking
The activities of advocates and their referred friends are tracked in a referral program. Rewards are
automatically provided to advocates and their referred friends when reward-eligible activities are
completed. You can use a Business API or a flow action to create records that track the activities of
advocates and their referred friends.
Voucher Redemption
Use the Redeem Voucher API to redeem the vouchers that advocates and their referred friends use.
Integrate the Redeem Voucher API with one or more of your external systems where vouchers are
redeemed. For example, you can integrate the API with the ecommerce site and POS system where
customers use their voucher.
Options to Extend Referral Marketing
Referral Marketing is prebuilt with a set of standard objects and an API to help admins and developers
extend Referral Marketing.
Advocate Enrollment
After marketing managers activate referral promotions, the marketing manager, the admin, and the
developer can decide how they want the brand’s advocates to join the referral promotions. For a
promotion, the brand can choose to either embed the promotion’s widget on a site or use a business API
to process advocate enrollments.
How Advocate Enrollments are Tracked in Referral Marketing
Each time a referral program advocate or a customer joins a referral promotion, the enrollment is
tracked by using a Transaction Journal record and a set of related records. An email is also sent to the
enrolled advocates.
Advocate Enrollment by Using Refer A Friend Widget
The Refer A Friend widget is available with every referral promotion and the marketing manager can
customize the widget based on the brand’s requirements. The widget lets advocates join the
promotion and refer their friends. The widget also lets new customers sign up with the brand, join the
promotion, and then refer their friends. You can embed the widget on Experience Cloud sites and on
external websites.
Advocate Enrollment by Using Business API
Use the Referral Advocate Enrollments Business API to enroll existing and new customers in referral
promotions. Integrate the API with any site or external system where customers can join the referral
promotion. For example, you can integrate the API with your brand’s ecommerce site or POS system.
Advocate Enrollment Without Person Account
When you don’t have person accounts enabled in your org, the process of enrolling advocates differs
from the standard procedure.
How Advocate Enrollments are Tracked in Referral Marketing
Each time a referral program advocate or a customer joins a referral promotion, the enrollment is tracked
by using a Transaction Journal record and a set of related records. An email is also sent to the enrolled

Send an Email to the Enrolled Advocate
If the marketing manager activated the Thank Advocates for Joining email for the referral promotion that
the advocate joined, the email is automatically sent to the advocate after they join the promotion. The
email contains the advocate’s unique referral link that they can share with their friends.
The Remind Advocates to Start Referring reminder email is sent to the advocates who didn’t refer their
friends yet if the marketing manager also activated the reminder email. The reminder email is sent after a
few days. The marketing manager decides the gap between the Thank Advocates for Joining email and
the Remind Advocates for Joining email when they design the promotion.
Choose How You Want to Enroll Advocates
Enroll new and existing customers and referral program advocates in a referral promotion in these ways:
•
Refer A Friend widget—The admin can embed the widget on an Experience Cloud site or an external
site. The widget also lets advocates send a referral email to their friends after they join the promotion.
•
Advocate Enrollment business API—The admin or the developer can integrate the API with an external
system where the brand’s customers or advocates can join the promotion.
Advocate Enrollment by Using Refer A Friend Widget
The Refer A Friend widget is available with every referral promotion and the marketing manager can
customize the widget based on the brand’s requirements. The widget lets advocates join the promotion
and refer their friends. The widget also lets new customers sign up with the brand, join the promotion,
and then refer their friends. You can embed the widget on Experience Cloud sites and on external
websites.

Embed Widget on Experience Cloud Site
After the marketing manager customizes the Refer A Friend widget for a promotion, the widget must be
activated. Activated widgets are available as FlexCard components on the Experience Cloud site builder.
Admins can embed the widget’s FlexCard on the brand’s Experience Cloud site. See Add a FlexCard to an
Experience Cloud Page.
Embed Widget on External Site
After the marketing manager customizes the Refer A Friend widget for a promotion, the widget must be
downloaded. The widget is downloaded as a FlexCard Lightning Web Component (LWC) and the
marketing manager can share the downloaded files with the admin.
The admin can use OmniOut to embed the widget on an external site. To learn how to embed widgets by
using OmniOut, see Add a FlexCard LWC to OmniOut.
Track Referral Emails Sent by Advocates from the Widget
After a customer or an advocate joins a referral promotion by using the Refer A Friend widget, they can
send referral emails to their friends. To learn how advocate referrals are tracked, see How Activities are
Tracked in Referral Marketing.
An advocate can send referral emails to 10 friends at a time by using the Refer A Friend widget. The
program manager can set a limit on the number of friends that the advocate can refer each day. For
example, if the limit is five, the advocate can send the referral email to only five friends in a day. If the
limit is 15, the advocate can send the referral email to ten friends first and then send the email to five
more friends.
Watch and Learn
To learn how to embed widgets on Experience Cloud sites and external sites, watch Embed Widgets

promotions. Integrate the API with any site or external system where customers can join the referral
promotion. For example, you can integrate the API with your brand’s ecommerce site or POS system.

Learn About the Advocate Enrollment Business API
To learn about the Advocate Enrollment Business API’s resource, request body, and response body, see
Referral Advocate Enrollments in the Referral Marketing Developer Guide.
Enroll Existing Referral Program Advocates
To enroll an advocate of your referral program in a promotion, run the API with the membership number
of the advocate. The advocate’s membership number is stored in the Membership Number field on the
advocate’s Loyalty Program Member record.
Enroll Existing Customers
To enroll an existing customer who isn’t an advocate of your referral program in a promotion, run the API
with the ID of the customer’s contact record.
Enroll New Customers
To enroll a person who hasn’t signed up with the brand and who doesn’t have a contact record in the org,
run the API with the person’s contact details.
Tip For new customers who are joining as advocates, you can also specify a unique membership
number. Use the membershipNumber field in the API request body to specify a unique
membership number that you want to provide to the advocate or that the advocate has specified. If
you don’t specify a membership number, an eight-character membership number is automatically
generated for the advocate.
Advocate Enrollment Without Person Account
When you don’t have person accounts enabled in your org, the process of enrolling advocates differs
from the standard procedure.
With no person accounts, the existing contacts in your org can sign up as advocates for your referral
promotions. New customers that don’t exist as contacts in your org can't sign up as advocates. Set up a
custom process to create Contact records to enroll in your company's referral promotions. You can also
execute the Referral Advocate Enrollment API to enroll customers in to a referral promotion.

=== PAGE 133 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
Referral Activity Tracking
The activities of advocates and their referred friends are tracked in a referral program. Rewards are
automatically provided to advocates and their referred friends when reward-eligible activities are
completed. You can use a Business API or a flow action to create records that track the activities of
advocates and their referred friends.
How Activities are Tracked in Referral Marketing
A referral promotion must track activities that advocates and their referred friends complete through
the promotion's stages. For activities in each stage, a set of records is created or updated, and emails
are sent to either the advocates or their referred friends.
Referral Event Business API
Use the Referral Event Business API to create tracking records for referral activities that advocates and
their referred friends complete during the last three stages of promotions. The API also automates the
issuing of rewards after advocates and their referred friends complete eligible activities. For each
activity, a transaction journal is created and other records are created or updated. Integrate the API
with any site or external website where advocates and their referred friends perform the activities. For
example, you can integrate the API with your ecommerce site, point of sale (POS), or customer portal.
Referral Event Action
Use the Process Referral Event action in Flow Builder to create tracking records for referral activities
that advocates and their referred friends complete during the last three stages of promotions. The
action also automates the issuing of rewards after advocates and their referred friends complete
eligible activities. For each activity, a transaction journal is created and other records are created or
updated. Use the additional elements in Flow Builder to decide the eligibility criteria for referral
activities. You can also add follow-up actions after the Process Referral action.
Orchestration of Extended Rewards
Use extended rewards to gain precise control over your referral programs. Dynamically adjust reward
values, control when extended rewards are issued, and communicate them clearly with customers.
Gain granular control over the events that trigger rewards. With extended rewards, you can integrate
with external platforms to deliver a wider range of rewards. After you activate a referral program with
extended rewards, understand how they are processed and connected with external systems.
Referral Activity Tracking Without Person Account
When you don’t have person accounts enabled in your org, the process of tracking activities differs
from the standard procedure.
How Activities are Tracked in Referral Marketing
A referral promotion must track activities that advocates and their referred friends complete through the
promotion's stages. For activities in each stage, a set of records is created or updated, and emails are sent
to either the advocates or their referred friends.

Understand How a Promotion's Template Determines How the Promotion's
Activities are Tracked
The stages of different promotions vary based on the promotion's template. A promotion's template
decides the names of the last three stages, at which stage advocates and their referred friends are
rewarded, and the activities that trigger rewards. The records to track each stage’s activities differ based
on when the promotion's template rewards the advocates and their referred friends.
The first two stages of each promotion template are locked. You can't track referral activities for the
Promotion Launched stage and the Advocate Refers Friend stage. During the Advocate Refers Friend
stage, advocates join the referral promotion. To learn more about advocate enrollment, see Advocate
Enrollment.
These records are created or updated when you create a referral promotion with the Refer a Friend
promotion template.

Ways to Track Referral Activities
You can set up a process to track referral activities in these ways:
•
Referral Event business API—The admin or the developer can integrate the API with external systems
where advocates can refer their friends or where referred friends can sign up and shop with the brand.
•
Process Referral Event action—The admin or the developer can add the action to an existing business
process. As part of this process, advocates can refer their friends and referred friends can sign up and
shop with the brand. The action is available for admins in Flow Builder and developers can access the
action as an invocable action or from Apex.
Referral Event Business API
Use the Referral Event Business API to create tracking records for referral activities that advocates and
their referred friends complete during the last three stages of promotions. The API also automates the
issuing of rewards after advocates and their referred friends complete eligible activities. For each activity,
a transaction journal is created and other records are created or updated. Integrate the API with any site
or external website where advocates and their referred friends perform the activities. For example, you
can integrate the API with your ecommerce site, point of sale (POS), or customer portal.
138

=== PAGE 143 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
About the Referral Event Business API
To learn more about the Referral Event Business API’s resource, request body, and response body, see
Referral Event in the Referral Marketing Developer Guide.
Stage 3
During the first and second stages, the promotion only interacts with the advocates. In the third stage,
advocates refer their friends. To track an advocate’s referral, run the API with these fields:
•
eventType —Specify the event type as Refer.
•
referralCode —Specify the code of the advocate who referred their friend and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of, separated by a hyphen.
•
activityDateTime —Specify the date and time when the advocate referred their friend.
•
firstName —Specify the first name of the referred friend.
•
lastName —Specify the last name of the referred friend.
•
email —Specify the email address of the referred friend.
If a contact exists for the friend in the org, specify the contact ID of the friend instead of the first name,
last name, and email address.
Stage 4
After advocates refer their friends in the third stage, the referred friends engage with the brand for the
first time. The ways of engagement can differ based on your business requirements or industry. To track a
referred friend engaging with the brand, run the API with these fields:
•
eventType —Specify the event type as Enrollment.
•
referralCode —Specify the code of the advocate who referred their friend and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of, separated by a hyphen.
•
contactId —Specify the ID of the friend’s Contact record.
•
activityDateTime —Specify the date and time when the friend signed up.
If a contact doesn’t exist for the friend, specify the first name, last name, and email address of the friend
instead of the contact ID.
139

=== PAGE 144 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
Stage 5
After referred friends engage with the brand for the first time, they must complete an activity. The activity
varies based on your promotion's goals and industry. To track the completion of an activity by a referred
friend, run the API with these fields:
•
eventType —Specify the event type as Purchase.
•
referralCode —Specify the code of the advocate who referred their friend and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of, separated by a hyphen.
•
contactId —Specify the ID of the friend’s contact record.
•
activityDateTime —Specify the date and time when the friend completed their first purchase.
If a contact doesn’t exist for the friend, specify the first name, last name, and email address of the friend
instead of the contact ID.
Tip To ensure that the Referral Event Business API doesn’t create duplicate contacts for advocates
and duplicate contacts and person accounts for referred friends, create matching rules and
duplicate rules on the Contact and Person Account objects.
See Also
Salesforce Help: Matching Rules and Duplicate Rules for Contacts and Person Accounts
Referral Event Action
Use the Process Referral Event action in Flow Builder to create tracking records for referral activities that
advocates and their referred friends complete during the last three stages of promotions. The action also
automates the issuing of rewards after advocates and their referred friends complete eligible activities.
For each activity, a transaction journal is created and other records are created or updated. Use the
additional elements in Flow Builder to decide the eligibility criteria for referral activities. You can also add
follow-up actions after the Process Referral action.

Orchestration of Extended Rewards
Use extended rewards to gain precise control over your referral programs. Dynamically adjust reward
values, control when extended rewards are issued, and communicate them clearly with customers. Gain
granular control over the events that trigger rewards. With extended rewards, you can integrate with
external platforms to deliver a wider range of rewards. After you activate a referral program with
extended rewards, understand how they are processed and connected with external systems.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
142

=== PAGE 147 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Extended rewards change how your company gives out incentives in referral programs. With extended
rewards, you can move beyond vouchers to offer cash back, gift cards, variable amounts, or delayed
payouts.
After a referral program offering extended rewards is activated and a referral event is triggered where
either the advocate or the referred friend is rewarded, an extended reward record is automatically
created with a Pending status.
Your company can apply custom logic to calculate or override the reward value. This custom logic can be
defined using various tools. For example, you can use decision tables to dynamically calculate or override
the reward value based on specific transaction attributes, or you can use the Data Processing Engine for
delayed payouts.
Although a Marketing Cloud Engagement journey is prepared for content delivery, the content is only
sent to the target audience after the reward value is finalized.
After the reward value is finalized, the status of the extended reward is changed to Issued, and the
journey associated with it is executed. As the reward value was changed, Marketing Cloud Engagement
emails are sent with the updated reward value. You can use resources like flows or APEX to integrate with
external rewards systems like rewards wallets or subscription management platforms.
Here are a few business scenarios where extended rewards can be used to adjust reward values at
runtime.

Referral Activity Tracking Without Person Account
When you don’t have person accounts enabled in your org, the process of tracking activities differs from
the standard procedure.
With no person accounts, the Referral Marketing system can’t create records to track the activities of
advocates and their referred friends. Set up a custom process to create or import Contact records for
new customers that help track the activities. You can also execute the Referral Event API to create
tracking records for referral activities.
145

=== PAGE 150 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Referral Processes
Voucher Redemption
Use the Redeem Voucher API to redeem the vouchers that advocates and their referred friends use.
Integrate the Redeem Voucher API with one or more of your external systems where vouchers are
redeemed. For example, you can integrate the API with the ecommerce site and POS system where
customers use their voucher.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Redeem Voucher Business API
To learn about the Redeem Voucher API’s resource, request body, and response body, see Redeem
Vouchers in the Referral Marketing Developer Guide.
Redeem Vouchers Issued to Advocates
To redeem a voucher that’s used by an advocate, run the API with the code of the redeemed voucher
and the advocate’s membership number or Loyalty Program Member ID.
Redeem Vouchers Issued to Referred Friends
To redeem a voucher that’s used by a referred friend, run the API with the code of the redeemed voucher
and the referred friend’s Contact ID.
Tip If advocates and their referred friends are issued a fixed value voucher that’s partially
redeemable, specify the amount that was redeemed. The amount remaining in the voucher is
automatically calculated and can be used in a subsequent purchase. After the voucher is partially
redeemed, the status of the voucher remains as Issued. If the redemption amount isn’t specified for
a partially redeemable voucher, the complete voucher amount is redeemed and the voucher status
is changed to Redeemed. If multiple currencies are enabled in the org, specify the currency that the
amount is redeemed in.
What Happens After Vouchers are Redeemed
Redemption Scenario What Happens
A single use voucher is redeemed The status of the voucher is changed to
Redeemed and the use date is updated to the
current date.

calculated.

current date. The redeemed amount is updated
with the value that was redeemed across the two
purchases and the remaining value is updated to
zero.
What Happens to Vouchers That Are Past Their Expiration Date
An automated process expires unredeemed and partially redeemed vouchers that are past their
expiration date daily. The automated process can expire up to two million vouchers in a day.
If your brand requires to expire more than two million vouchers in a day, the admin can design a batch
Apex job to expire the vouchers that the automated process didn’t expire.

Referral Marketing is prebuilt with a set of standard objects and an API to help admins and developers
extend Referral Marketing.

Migrate Data from One Org to Another
To run referral promotions, loyalty program processes are automatically created behind the scenes. After
you configure a promotion in an org, use the LoyaltyProgramSetup Metadata API to move the
processes from the org to another org.

Referral Marketing Developer Guide: Introduction to Referral Marketing
Manage a Referral Program
After advocates join the brand’s referral promotion and start referring their friends, marketing managers
can track the progress of each referral.
Manage Advocates
After a brand launches their referral promotion, marketing managers can review the details of the
advocates who are part of the referral program and can add advocates to referral promotions.
Manage Activities
While marketing managers review the performance of a referral program and its promotions, they can
review the activities completed by advocates and their referred friends.
Track Advocate Count for Promotions
After an advocate joins a promotion, a Loyalty Program Member Promotion record is automatically
created to track the advocate's participation in the promotion. From the Loyalty Program Member
Promotion related list on a promotion, marketing managers can track the count of advocates who
have joined the promotion and their details. The marketing managers can use a promotion's advocate
count as a key performance indicator of the promotion. The Loyalty Program Member Promotion
related list also helps marketing managers find out the promotion's active advocate count.
Track Referrals
Referral records help marketing managers track the progress of an advocate’s referral. When an
advocate’s referral progresses across the promotion stages, the Referral record is also updated to the
current stage.
Track Issued Vouchers
Vouchers issued to advocates are associated with the advocate's contact and vouchers issued to
referred friends are associated with the friend's person account. Marketing managers can keep a track
of the vouchers issued to a person by viewing their contact or person account.
View Promotion Configuration
View the detailed configuration of a referral promotion with one click. Users with read-only access to
referral entities can quickly view the promotion configuration. Promotion owners can review the
promotion details and determine the changes they want to make without deactivating the promotion.
Plan Promotions by Using the Promotion Calendar
Marketing managers and business executives can visualize the brand’s referral promotions on the
promotion calendar. The calendar lists the brand’s referral promotions and events, so the marketing
managers can check whether promotions are planned during company and social events. Like any
other calendar, marketing managers can move across date ranges to see the promotions that are
running or that are scheduled. Along with the marketing managers, business executives get a high-
level view of the brand’s promotions, easily find white spaces where new promotions can be added,
148

Referral Marketing Manage a Referral Program
and identify duplicate promotions.

After a brand launches their referral promotion, marketing managers can review the details of the
advocates who are part of the referral program and can add advocates to referral promotions.

managers can check whether promotions are planned during company and social events. Like any other

that are scheduled. Along with the marketing managers, business executives get a high-level view of the
brand’s promotions, easily find white spaces where new promotions can be added, and identify duplicate
promotions.

162

=== PAGE 167 ===

Likelihood of Referrals recipe and includes data only for advocate members.
The dashboard shows the average likelihood of advocates referring their friends, the number of referrals,
and the unique number of advocates by state, city, and referral likelihood score. Use the charts to view
the number of advocates by state, predictions based on membership duration, and transaction details
by range. In the Advocate Transaction Details by Ranges chart, each metric tile represents a specific
range of values.
The metric tiles with the darkest shade represent advocates with the highest possibility to refer. The tile
with the darkest shade (Quartile 1) indicates higher referral potential and must be prioritized. The
second tier, represented by the next darker shade, includes advocates who exhibit a strong possibility to
refer and make up a significant portion of the member base. The metric ranges in the chart serve as
filters and you can identify and categorize advocates or contacts based on their possibility to refer.
Note Amounts of 0 in Transaction Journal records indicate that the transaction data from the
external systems requires updating. The Referral system retrieves transactions from these systems
and doesn't record them independently.

Likelihood Score for Referral Marketing Model Card
The Predict Customer Likelihood of Referring model predicts the likelihood of referral program members
referring to their contacts. The model generates a score between 1 and 100, with 100 indicating the
highest probability of referral.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Model Details
The Predict Customer Likelihood of Referring model is trained and deployed in the Salesforce Referral
Cloud environment. The Get Predicted Likelihood of Referrals recipe generates the referral predictions,
which are displayed on the Advocates' Likelihood of Referring dashboard. The dashboard shows the
average likelihood of advocates referring, the number of referrals, the unique number of contacts, and
the percentage of advocates who are part of a referral program.
•
Model Input: Predict Customer Likelihood of Referring analyzes each referral program to derive these
inputs. The model doesn’t use demographic data or other data purchased from third-party data
163

=== PAGE 168 ===
Referral Marketing Get Predictions about Advocates’ Likelihood of Referring
providers.
- ReferredPartyId, MemberStatus, MemberType, and ReferredById contain customer information,
including membership status and type.
- Enrollment Date and Creation date provide insights into when customers enrolled or were created
in the system for tracking customer acquisition trends.
- Id, TransactionAmount, and ActivityDate capture unique identifiers (IDs), transaction amounts, and
activity dates to analyze customer behavior and transaction history.
- TotalAmount and Product2Id provide the total transaction amount and product identifiers for
assessing customer value and product performance.
•
Person or Organization: Salesforce Referral Cloud
•
Model Date and Version
- October 2023
- Minor changes can occur throughout the release
- Major changes can occur and are communicated via release notes
•
Model Type: Classification
Intended Use
The Predict Customer Likelihood of Referring model is intended for referral program managers. Anything
other than the primary use case is out of scope and not recommended.
Metrics
Einstein evaluates model performance metrics to ensure and improve the quality of the model. The
model performance metrics include the model fitness score based on the AUC curve, GINI, Log Loss,
and the data richness score.
Training Data
You have a customized version of the model that’s trained on your data alone, unless you’ve opted in to
use global model data. Data from another Salesforce customer doesn’t affect the behavior of your data.
The initial development of the model is validated with a representative set of pilot customers’ data, but
all model training occurs only on your data.
Ethical Considerations
To avoid bias and other ethical risks, the Predict Customer Likelihood of Referring model doesn’t include
demographic data.
You are responsible for interpreting the Einstein insights, and you must be aware of any assumptions that
you make when acting on the model’s insights. However, adverse outcomes are possible due to model
error.

For example, a marketer opts not to send referral incentives-related information to a loyal customer
based on an inaccurate model prediction that the customer is unlikely to make referrals. This decision
leads to missed opportunities for the customer and impacts the effectiveness of the referral program.
Refresh Cadence
The model doesn’t have an established refresh schedule, but you can schedule a score refresh based on
your requirements.
Questions or Comments
Send questions or comments about the model to mce-support@salesforce.com.

whether the data point is part of the training set. Refer to the image for an example.

Dashboard
The Contact Likelihood of Referring dashboard shows predictions generated by the Get Referral
Likelihood Predictions recipe and includes only the non-advocate contacts data.
The dashboard shows the average likelihood of contacts referring, the total contacts, the unique number
of contacts by state, city, and the likelihood of referring score. Use the charts to see the number of
contacts by state, prediction based on the duration since contact creation and the last transaction date,
and how the prediction scores vary based on the values for various transaction metrics.

Build Solutions Based on Your Requirements
Every company has their own business needs and marketing strategies. Referral Marketing is flexible and
you can extend it to meet your business needs. Review these common solutions that you can build with
Referral Marketing.
Integrate Referral Marketing with B2C Commerce
Use a reference implementation to understand how to integrate Referral Marketing with B2C
Commerce.
Offer Gift Cards to Advocates and Friends
Integrate Referral Marketing with gift card solutions to offer your advocates and their referred friends
gift cards instead of vouchers.
Run Referral Promotions As Part of the Company's Loyalty Program
In orgs that have both Loyalty Management and Referral Marketing, marketing managers can run
referral promotions as part of the company's loyalty program. Your company can run a referral
promotion that's targeted towards members of the company's loyalty program. With loyalty program
members as advocates of your referral promotion, you can generate high-quality referrals from
customers who are already trust your brand. The referral promotion increases the engagement of
loyalty program members with the brand by offering members rewards for the referrals.
Integrate Referral Marketing with B2C Commerce
Use a reference implementation to understand how to integrate Referral Marketing with B2C Commerce.
Important The Referral Marketing for Commerce is a Non-GA Service. Such Non-GA Service is
subject to the terms and conditions of an existing fully executed Unified Partner Research
Agreement (“UPRA”), or in the absence of a signed UPRA, the UPRA available online at Terms and
Agreements.

Automatically Add the Cartridge
11.. Set up these environment variables in your B2C Commerce site:
Variable Description
SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID The client ID used for authentication. The client
ID is available in Account Manager.
SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET The client secret used for authentication. The
client secret is the password you created when
creating your client ID.

=== PAGE 185 ===
Referral Marketing Build Solutions Based on Your Requirements
Variable Description
SFCC_HOSTNAME The alias of your sandbox.
SFCC_CODE_VERSION The code version for which you want to add the
cartridge. You can find the code version of your
site on Adminstration | Code Deployment in
Account Manager.
SFCC_SITE_IDS The ID of the B2C Commerce site to add the
cartridge to.
22.. If dw.json is available in your referral-marketing-for-commerce/src/sfcc folder, delete it.
33.. On your CLI, run these commands:
aa.. npm ci
bb.. npm run compile:js && npm run compile:scss
cc.. npm run -s deploy:auto
Example For MacOS and Linux, here's an example environment variable setting:
export SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID=xxxxxxa1-xxx2-xxx3-xxx4-xxxxxxxxx5 && \
export SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET=samplepassword && \
export SFCC_HOSTNAME=sandbox-01-inside-the-realm.cloudkicks.net && \
export SFCC_CODE_VERSION=version1
export SFCC_SITE_IDS="sampleSiteID"
For Windows, here's an example environment variable setting:
set SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID=xxxxxxa1-xxx2-xxx3-xxx4-xxxxxxxxx5 &&
set SFCC_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET=samplepassword &&
set SFCC_HOSTNAME=sandbox-01-inside-the-realm.cloudkicks.net &&
set SFCC_CODE_VERSION=version1
set SFCC_SITE_IDS=sampleSiteID

New and existing customers of your B2C Commerce site can join the referral program. Customers new
to your site can join the referral program when creating an account on the site. Existing customers can
join the referral program from their My Account page. Customers can review the terms and conditions
of the referral program before joining the referral program.

Tip Admins of your B2C Commerce site can modify the terms and conditions of the referral program

After a customer joins the referral program, an email is sent informing that their account was edited.

member in the email.
How Does Enrollment Work?
When a new or existing customer joins your referral program, these automated processes are run:
Sequence Process
1
The Referral Marketing B2C Commerce: Create or
Update Member's Contact Record flow is run in
your Salesforce org. The flow checks if a Contact
record exists in the org for the member. If a record
doesn't exist, the flow creates a Contact record for
the member and either creates or assigns an
Account record to the member’s Contact record. If
a Contact record exists for the member, the
member’s Contact record is updated with the
186

=== PAGE 191 ===
Referral Marketing Build Solutions Based on Your Requirements
Sequence Process
member’s details.
After identifying or creating a Contact record for
the member, the flow checks if the member
already has a Referral Program Member record. If
a record doesn't exist, a new Referral Program
Member record is created for the member. If a
Referral Program Member record exists, the
member’s details are updated in the Referral
Program Member record.
2 The Referral Marketing B2C Commerce: Create
Transaction Journals on Member Enrolment flow
is run to create an Enrollment type Transaction
Journal record for the member and runs the
B2CReferralCreditPoints Apex class to credit 50
points to the member.
3
These Referral Program Member record details are
added to the customer's record in Business
Manager:
•
Status of the membership
•
ID of the customer's Referral Program Member
record
•
Referral program membership number
•
Name of the customer's referral program
•
ID of the customer's Referral Program record

Members can also view the details of their activities on the My Activities page of the B2C Commerce site.

My Activities
The activity information on My Activities is provided by the Referral Management B2C Commerce: Get
Member's Transaction and Ledgers flow that's available in the provided org.
Members can view the details of their activities, sourced from the member's Transaction Journal records.
Members can view the number of points that they accrued or redeemed for each activity. Members can
also view the transactions that are created for points adjustments and the transactions that are created
to credit points for non-purchase activities, such as receiving an enrollment bonus.
Note The activities list also contains transaction journals that haven't credited points to or debited
points from the member's points balance. For example, transaction journals that are associated with
products for which members don't accrue points.
Promotions
Members can view the promotions that are applicable for a product or its category on the product's page
on the B2C Commerce site.

Voucher Redemption for Order Payment
Referral program members can use their issued vouchers to pay for orders. Members can pay for an
order with vouchers, and other payment methods.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Note Before members use points and vouchers to place orders, admins must ensure that your
referral program points and vouchers are active payment methods for the site in Business Manager.
Admins must also ensure that a value is specified in the Cost per Unit field of the referral program's
non-qualifying Referral Program Currency record. This value is also stored in the customer's record
on the site.
Redeem Vouchers for an Order
Members can view the vouchers that they can apply for an order on the Redeem Vouchers section of the
payment page. The B2C Commerce site admin defines the number of vouchers members can redeem
for an order.
After a member applies a voucher, the member can view the value that's deducted from their payable
amount in the order summary. By default, the available voucher value is redeemed for an order.
Review Payment Details
After an order is placed, members' can view the points redeemed and the voucher value used in the
order receipt.
B2C Commerce admins can view the points redeemed and the voucher value used for an order by
reviewing the payment details of an order in Business Manager.

Limitations of Referral Marketing's Integration with B2C Commerce
The sample implementation of integrating Referral Marketing with B2C Commerce has some limitations.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Integration Limitations
On the B2C Commerce site, members can:
•
Enroll into only one referral promotion
•
Redeem only Fixed Value type vouchers
•
View but not enroll into promotions that require enrollment
•
Redeem only up to five vouchers for an order
•
Add up to 75 items in an order
Why Are Visitors Finding It Difficult to Create an Account on the Site?
Ensure that site admins have set up the password, phone number, and email ID policies for your site.
Why Does Member Enrollment Fail in the B2C Commerce Site Sandbox?
This happens when the system is inactive for a while. The system can be made active by calling one of
the site APIs. This issue doesn’t impact production orgs.
190

=== PAGE 195 ===
Referral Marketing Build Solutions Based on Your Requirements
Why Doesn't Members' Activities Page List Their Activities?
This happens when the required journal subtypes aren't associated with the members' Transaction
Journal records in your Salesforce org. Associate all of your members' new and existing Transaction
Journals with the applicable journal subtypes. For example, the transaction journal that's created when a
customer joins the referral program must be associated with the Enrollment journal subtype.
Do the API Calls Made by the Integration Count as Part of the Org's Daily
Allocation?
Yes. The API calls made by the integration count as part of your org's 24-hour period API allocation.
Do I Receive Emails if a Batch Management Job’s Run or a Data Processing
Engine Definition’s Run Fails?
To track the status of your Batch Management job and Data Processing Engine definition runs, use
Monitor Workflow Services in Setup. Monitor Workflow Services allows you to check the details of each
run of a Batch Management job or Data Processing Engine definition.

Run Referral Promotions As Part of the Company's Loyalty Program
In orgs that have both Loyalty Management and Referral Marketing, marketing managers can run referral
promotions as part of the company's loyalty program. Your company can run a referral promotion that's
targeted towards members of the company's loyalty program. With loyalty program members as
advocates of your referral promotion, you can generate high-quality referrals from customers who are
already trust your brand. The referral promotion increases the engagement of loyalty program members
with the brand by offering members rewards for the referrals.

Manage Data Protection and Privacy for Referral Marketing
When brands run their referral programs, they must comply with local and global data protection and
privacy regulations. As part of your brand’s referral program strategy, decide how you want to delete,
export, archive, restrict access, manage consent, and restrict the processing of customer data stored as
part of the referral programs.
Data Deletion for Referral Marketing
Delete the personal data of customers when it’s necessary to comply with data protection and privacy
regulations. Determine a plan of action for complying with the regulations that apply to your company.
Consent Management for Referral Marketing
Honor and respect the wishes of your customers when they request only specific forms of contact
from your company or when they opt out of certain types of data-sharing. We provide details to help
you determine the best way to comply with the data protection and privacy regulations that apply to
your company.
Restrict Data Processing for Referral Marketing
When situations require you to do so, prevent the processing of your customers’ data. We give
guidance to help you restrict the forms of data processing. That way, you can work toward complying
with the laws that are important to your company.
Data Access and Export for Referral Marketing
When your customers request it, prepare and pack up the data that you received from them to comply
with data protection and privacy regulations. Determine the best way to work toward complying with
the regulations that apply to your company.
Data Deletion for Referral Marketing
Delete the personal data of customers when it’s necessary to comply with data protection and privacy

Referral Marketing
B2B Referral Management helps your brand run referral programs with evergreen and time-bound
promotions for your channel partners. Channel managers can design and launch referral promotions
within minutes. B2B Referral Management takes care of the rest with its inbuilt automations by
rewarding advocates and their referred parties.
Learn About B2B Referral Management
Learn about the key terms and roles in B2B Referral Management. Explore the B2B Referral
Management data model and the referral program workflow.
Set Up B2B Referral Management
Set up capabilities that enable channel managers to design and run referral programs. Set up rules to
prevent duplicate records and protect against malicious activities. Enable channel managers and
service representatives to track referral rewards issued to advocates and their referred parties.
Design a Referral Program
Channel managers can use a guided flow to design and launch a referral program and its promotions
by completing a few simple steps.
Configure Processes
After channel managers create the referral program and add its promotions, the admin or the
developer can configure the everyday processes. The processes include advocate enrollment and
activity tracking.
Manage a B2B Referral Program
After advocates join the brand’s referral promotion and start referring another businesses, channel
managers can track the progress of each referral.

=== PAGE 211 ===
Referral Marketing Learn About B2B Referral Management
Ecosystem management.
The following scenarios illustrate how referrals can be generated through these channels:
Customer Referrals
Customer referrals occur when your existing customers recommend your business to other potential
customers, helping to drive new business opportunities. For example, Intel, a leading technology
company, has a strong relationship with Dell, a major computer manufacturer. Intel is aware that
Seagate, another technology company, produces high-quality laptop batteries. Intel decides to refer
Seagate to Dell, suggesting that Dell consider Seagate as a supplier for their laptop batteries.
Partner Referrals
Partner referrals occur when your existing business partners recommend your business to other potential
customers. For example, IBM, a leading technology and consulting company, has a strategic partnership
with Tableau, a data visualization platform. IBM also has a strong relationship with a major financial
institution. IBM recognizes that Tableau's data visualization tools could significantly enhance the financial
institution's data analysis and reporting capabilities. IBM decides to refer Tableau to the financial
institution, suggesting that they consider Tableau as an addon to their data analysis feature.
B2B Referral Management Data Model
Learn about the objects in the B2B Referral Management data model.

Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing

Members or Partner Ecosystem Management - Login. Learn more about Referral Marketing with Partner
Ecosystem management.

Use these objects to create a referral program and its promotions.

Loyalty Program
Stores information about referral programs.
Voucher Definition
Stores information about voucher templates that are used to issue vouchers to advocates or to
their referred party. Each voucher definition is associated with a referral program.
Promotion Template
Stores information about the reusable referral promotion templates that are used to create
promotions.
Promotion Stage Template
Stores information about the stages of a promotion template that are used to define when
advocates and their referred parties are rewarded and the activities that rewards are offered for.
Promotion
Stores the configuration and detailed information of referral promotions. Each promotion is
associated with a referral program.
Promotion Stage
Stores information about the stages of referral promotions.
Extended Reward Definition

B2B Referral Management provides a journal type that you can use to track all referral activities.
You can’t extend or customize the Journal Type object or the Referral journal type.

Stores information about the subtype of referral activities that you create transaction journals for.
Product

example, you can either reward an advocate when they refer a business or reward them when the
referred party signs up using the advocate's referral link. You can't reward advocates and their referred
parties again. You can only reward a referred party when they have an account record.

Unique Referral Count
In B2B Referral Management, a unique referral is represented by the unique combination of the
advocate, referred business, and the active promotion associated with the referral. When a unique
referral record is created, the referral count is increases. The referral count isn't decreased if the referral
doesn't convert into opportunity.

Duplicate Rule and Matching Rule Configuration
In the B2B Referral Management org, create two matching rules for Account and Lead. In the criteria for
both matching rules, select Email as the field and Exact as the match method. After you create the
matching rules, create two duplicate rules for Account and Lead. Relate the duplicate rules to their
corresponding matching rules. The duplicate rules and their corresponding matching rules together
prevent businesses and their referred parties from signing up with the brand multiple times by using the
same email address.
You can also add actions and alert text that informs the person who is trying to sign up that they already
have an account with the brand.
Tip If your brand wants to run additional checks before creating account and lead records, you can
add the checks in the matching rules and duplicate rules.

Loyalty Program Page Layout
Update the standard and custom Loyalty Program page layout to include the Type and Subtype field. The
Type field identifies whether a record represents a loyalty program or a referral promotion. The Type field
comes with these values by default:
•
Referral—Added to the org by the B2B Referral Management license
•
Loyalty—Added to the org by the Loyalty Management license
The Subtype field identifies whether a record represents a B2B or B2C referral promotion. The Subtype
field comes with these values by default:
•
Business to Business—Added to the org by the B2B Referral Management license
•
Business to Customer—Added to the org by the Referral Marketing license
If users create a Loyalty Program record in an org where B2B Referral Management, Loyalty Management,
and Referral Marketing are enabled, the Type field of the record is automatically set to Loyalty.
Promotion Page Layout
Update the standard and custom Promotion page layouts to include the Promotion Code field. In B2B
Referral Management, channel managers use a unique code for each referral promotion. The code
uniquely identifies each promotion and the promotion that the referral activities belong to.
The promotion code is optional in Loyalty Management. Loyalty program managers can use the code to
uniquely identify loyalty promotions.
B2B Referral Management supports leveraging Loyalty IDs generated externally as Advocate Referral
Codes. An advocate referral code is a combination of the loyalty ID and the promotion code.When
processing advocate and referred party referral activities within the context of a referral promotion, the
referral events are processed using this referral code,
If a company wants their advocates to use their unique advocate ID, they must programmatically identify
the promotion context and append the referral promotion code when processing Referral events. This
ensures referral events are processed accurately in the referral promotions' context, and the correct
referral rewards are issued to advocates and their referred parties.

=== PAGE 230 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
How Referral Programs and Promotions Work Together
Brands run referral programs to encourage their partners and existing business customers to refer new
businesses. The timing of these programs can change depending on who they want to reach and when
they plan to contact advocates.
A referral program can include many different promotions, each designed for specific purposes.
Companies can set up promotions that run all the time (evergreen) or for a set period (time-bound).
These promotions can target specific partner groups or all of them.
Example Cloud Kicks wants to run an evergreen promotion, offering a $1000 discount for their
business partners and their referred parties. They also want to run two time-bound promotions: one
during the company's anniversary month and another on December 31 and January 31. The
channel manager creates one referral program and adds three promotions to it. The evergreen
promotion has a start date but no end date. The company anniversary promotion runs for a month,
and the year-end promotion starts on December 31 and ends on January 31.
Example Example Cloud Kicks wants to run a referral program for their business partners in France
and Canada. For France, they want to reward the partners and their referred party with a 10%
discount voucher. For Canada, Cloud Kicks wants to provide a 15% discount to the partners and a
10% voucher to the referred parties. In this case, Cloud Kicks can run two promotions, one for each
country.
Example Example Cloud Kicks wants to run a referral program that consists of an evergreen
promotion for all its business partners and a time-bound promotion for a specific partner group. For
the evergreen promotion, the partner manager selects a start date but doesn't select an end date or
a target audience. For the time-bound promotion, the partner manager selects a start date, an end
date, and a campaign that consists of the promotion's target audience. Cloud Kicks launches an
evergreen referral program for its entire network of channel partners, the evergreen promotion
offers a standard 5% commission on all successful referrals.
Create a Referral Program
The cornerstone of a referral strategy is the referral program. After setting up a referral program,
channel managers can manage and implement all aspects of their referral strategy from the referral
program.
Add Rewards
Incentivize advocates and their referred parties to engage with your brand by adding rewards to your
referral program. Channel managers can include rewards like vouchers and payout commissions that
resonate with their audience. They can add multiple reward types within a referral program, tailored
for both advocates and their referred parties. If a referral program includes several promotions, each
can offer its own unique set of rewards to create a personalized experience.
Add Advocates
Advocates of a referral program are the partners who are willing to refer your brand to another
businesses. Channel managers can either add all partners as advocates or add a select set of partners
to the referral program. If the number of partners to be added is small, partner managers can add the
226

=== PAGE 231 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
advocates one by one. Or, they can work with the admin to set up a process that adds all the
advocates simultaneously.
Promotion Template
Promotion templates determine promotion configuration. Use promotion templates to define stage
names, the stages at which advocates and their referred parties are rewarded, and the activities that
trigger rewards. Every promotion uses a promotion template. Before creating a promotion, decide
whether to use an existing template or create a unique one.
Create a Promotion
Promotions are the primary vehicle that run your referral program. Channel managers can design
different types of promotions with varying duration, audience, rewards, and stages.
Create a Referral Program
The cornerstone of a referral strategy is the referral program. After setting up a referral program, channel
managers can manage and implement all aspects of their referral strategy from the referral program.

Create Voucher Definition
Channel managers can create voucher definitions to incentivize advocates and their referred parties
with diverse rewards. They can add multiple vouchers to a referral program, offering different reward
types to advocates and their referred parties. Each referral promotion within a program can feature its
own unique set of vouchers, enhancing engagement and driving conversions.
Create Extended Reward Definitions
Channel managers can design diverse reward types for the company's referral program, including
payout comissions for both advocates and referred parties. With extended rewards, channel managers
get the flexibility to adjust reward values at runtime and control when rewards are issued. Use services
like Flows or Apex to define processes for integrating with external downstream rewarding systems.

Here are a few other key fields to consider when you create voucher definitions:
•
Effective Date—Select the date from when the voucher definition can be used to issue vouchers.
•
Time-Based Voucher Period— Select if you want the vouchers issued by the definition to expire at a
specific time.
- For fixed date type vouchers, you can specify the effective and expiration date time.
- For period type vouchers, you can specify the effective date time and specify the expiration period
in minutes, hours, or days.
•
Cost Per Voucher—Enter the liability that the company incurs each time a voucher is issued using the
definition.
•
Partial Redeemable—Select to let advocates and the referred parties use the voucher across multiple
purchases. This option is available only for fixed value vouchers.
•
Code Prefix, Code Suffix, and Autogenerated Code Length—Enter the prefix, suffix, and length of the
voucher code. The prefix and the suffix are used in the unique automatically generated voucher code,
and the length determines the voucher code length. If you don’t specify any of these values, a unique
eight-character code is generated for each issued voucher. Advocates and the referred parties use their
voucher code to redeem their voucher.
11.. On the Voucher Definitions related list of your referral program, click New.
22.. Define your voucher definition, and select Active.
33.. Save your changes.

- Name: Refer and Earn $10,000
- Type: Fixed Value
- Expiration Type: Period
- Expiration Period: 4
- Expiration Period Unit: Months
- Effective Date: July 14, 2025
- Code Prefix: PRE10
- Autogenerated Code Length: 10
•
Voucher definition for referred party:
- Name: Join us and get 15% off
- Type: Discount Percentage
- Expiration Type: Period
- Expiration Period: 4
- Expiration Period Unit: Months
- Effective Date: July 14, 2025
- Code Prefix: RFJ10
- Autogenerated Code Length: 12
Create Extended Reward Definitions
Channel managers can design diverse reward types for the company's referral program, including payout
comissions for both advocates and referred parties. With extended rewards, channel managers get the
flexibility to adjust reward values at runtime and control when rewards are issued. Use services like Flows
or Apex to define processes for integrating with external downstream rewarding systems.

Add Advocates
Advocates of a referral program are the partners who are willing to refer your brand to another
businesses. Channel managers can either add all partners as advocates or add a select set of partners to
the referral program. If the number of partners to be added is small, partner managers can add the
advocates one by one. Or, they can work with the admin to set up a process that adds all the advocates
simultaneously.

Promotion Template
Promotion templates determine promotion configuration. Use promotion templates to define stage
names, the stages at which advocates and their referred parties are rewarded, and the activities that
trigger rewards. Every promotion uses a promotion template. Before creating a promotion, decide
whether to use an existing template or create a unique one.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, and Unlimited Editions with Partner Ecosystem Management -
Members or Partner Ecosystem Management - Login. Learn more about Referral Marketing with Partner
Ecosystem management.
Default Promotion Template
B2B Referral Management provides a promotion template by default: Refer a Lead. This template isn't
available for channel managers to view or customize. Here's how the Refer a Lead promotion template is
configured:
Stage Name What Happens At This Stage
Promotion Launched Advocates are invited to join the promotion.
Advocate Joins Promotion Advocates join the promotion.
Advocate Submits Referral Advocates refer a business.
Referral Qualifies The referral qualifies as a potential business
customer.

Custom Promotion Templates
From the Promotion Templates related list on a referral program, you can view the promotion templates
already created. If none of the promotion templates work for your promotion, you can go ahead and
create a promotion template. After you create a promotion template, other channel managers and you
can reuse the template to create similar promotions.
Here are a few advantages of creating a promotion template:
•
Change the stage names as per the needs of your promotion.
•
Choose whether you want to reward both advocates and their referred parties, either, or none of
them.
•
Select the activity that advocates and their referred parties get rewards for.
•
Add extended rewards such as payout commission for advocates and referrals.
You can reward advocates and their referred party only one time each in the promotion's journey.

Here's how the last three stages are designed in most referral promotions:
•
Third stage—Advocates refer a business and a lead account is created for the referred party.
•
Fourth stage—Referred party qualifies as a potential business customer.
•
Fifth stage— The opportunity is closed or won.

brand requirements. In software industry, the journey can close when the referred party signs a service

complete during the stage. For example, name the stage Initial Onboarding Complete if you want
the referred party to complete the onboarding on the fifth stage.

B2B Referral Promotion Prerequisites
Before channel managers design a referral promotion, they must ensure that all the information that's

=== PAGE 243 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
B2B Referral Management Strategy
Every brand crafts its referral program uniquely to align with its specific requirements. B2B Referral
Management helps businesses design and manage multiple promotions simultaneously or one
promotion at a time based on the brand’s marketing strategy. Brands can also customize each
promotion's stages, define rewards, and target specific audiences to perfectly fit their unique B2B
objectives.
Promotion Audience
Referral promotions can be targeted either towards your entire partner base or towards specific
partner groups. Before you use the Referral Promotion guided flow to design a promotion, decide the
promotion’s target audience. If you want to target a specific partner group, you can filter the target
audience by using a campaign.
Eligible Activities for Promotions
A promotion rewards advocates and their referred parties when an eligible activity is completed.
Before you create a referral promotion, decide the promotion's eligible activities for advocates and
their referred parties. Eligible activities are represented as journal subtypes in Salesforce.
Promotion Rewards
Based on the promotion template that you want to use for your promotion, decide the rewards that
you want to offer as part of the promotion. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and
their referred parties, then decide whether you want to give the same reward to advocates and their
referred parties, or different rewards.
Common Business Requirements for B2B Referral Promotions
Before you create referral promotions, map some of the most common business requirements to the
prerequisites for creating a promotion.

Management helps businesses design and manage multiple promotions simultaneously or one
promotion at a time based on the brand’s marketing strategy. Brands can also customize each
promotion's stages, define rewards, and target specific audiences to perfectly fit their unique B2B
objectives.

Segment Target Audience by Using Campaign
You can also filter your promotion’s target audience by using campaigns. In a campaign, add the
accounts who you want to include as the promotion’s target audience.
To learn how to create campaigns and add accounts as campaign members, see Working with
Campaigns and Manage Campaign Members.
Important To create a campaign to filter accounts, ask your admin to select the Marketing User
permission in your User record.
What Happens if the Target Audience is Filtered Outside Salesforce
You can create a campaign and then work with your admin to:
•
Map the filtered target audience to the accounts in the org
•
Add the filtered accounts as members by using reports or the Data Import Wizard
What Happens After Segments or Campaigns are Created
After you create campaigns, you can select campaign members as a promotion’s target audience in the
Rewards and Limits step of the Referral Promotion Guided Setup.
Eligible Activities for Promotions
A promotion rewards advocates and their referred parties when an eligible activity is completed. Before
you create a referral promotion, decide the promotion's eligible activities for advocates and their referred
241

=== PAGE 246 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
parties. Eligible activities are represented as journal subtypes in Salesforce.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, and Unlimited Editions with Partner Ecosystem Management -
Members or Partner Ecosystem Management - Login. Learn more about Referral Marketing with Partner
Ecosystem management.
Journal Type and Journal Subtype Usage
•
Journal type—Used to identify activities that belong to advocates and their referred parties.
•
Journal subtype—Used to uniquely identify the type of activity completed by advocates and their
referred parties.
Default Journal Type and Journal Subtype
B2B Referral Management comes with one journal type: Referral. There’s also a set of journal subtypes
associated with the Referral journal type by default.
•
Advocate Enrollment—Used to identity an activity where an advocate has joined a promotion.
You can't reward advocates for joining a promotion.
•
Referral Lead Creation—Used to identify an activity where an advocate refers a business and a lead
record is created.
•
Referral Qualification—Used to identify an activity where the referred lead qualifies.
•
Advocate Reward—Used to identify the activity where the referral promotion rewards the advocate.
•
Referred Party Reward—Used to identify the activity where the referral promotion rewards the referred
party.
Tip To view the journal types and subtypes that are available in your org, you can access the list
views from the App Launcher.
Eligible Activities of Your Promotion
Apart from the Advocate Enrollment journal subtype, you can use any of the other journal subtypes to
identify the activities for which you want to reward advocates and their referred parties.
The journal subtypes that are provided by default don't always relate to the activities that you want to
qualify for rewards. You can create journal subtypes and name them based on the activities you want to
qualify for rewards. The journal subtypes that you create must be associated with the Referral journal
type.
242

=== PAGE 247 ===

Example A commercial cleaning service company wants to reward partner real estate management
companies for referring new building customers, and also for signing multi-year contracts with their
referred party. For these two activities, the partner manager creates two journal subtypes: New
Building Referral Secured and Referred Building Signs Multi-Year Contract.
Example A digital marketing agency wants to incentivize its current partners to refer new
businesses, and also to reward those new businesses for signing up for a comprehensive annual
marketing package. For these two distinct actions, the agency's partner manager creates two journal
subtypes: Client Referral of New Business and New Client Annual Package Enrollment.
Promotion Rewards
Based on the promotion template that you want to use for your promotion, decide the rewards that you
want to offer as part of the promotion. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and their
referred parties, then decide whether you want to give the same reward to advocates and their referred
parties, or different rewards.

=== PAGE 251 ===

In the last step of the guided flow, review the journey of the advocates and their referred party in the
promotion. Verify your promotion's duration, target audience, and rewards. If something isn't right,
you can go back and make the required changes.
Promotion Definition
In the first step of the guided flow, define the key attributes of the promotion.

Define these key attributes of the promotion:
Attribute Function
Name The name of the referral promotion that’s used in your customer-
facing communication.
Description
Your brand’s internal goals or objectives for the referral promotion.
Description is an optional attribute.
Promotion duration
The start and end dates of the promotion determine how long the
promotion runs. During the duration of the promotion:
•
Advocates can join the referral program and refer another
businesses
•
Businesses can sign up with the brand
•
Advocates and referred parties can be rewarded
If you’re creating an evergreen promotion, don’t specify an end
date.
Promotion code
An advocate’s referral code consists of the promotion code and the
advocate’s unique code.
Referred parties use their advocate’s referral code to sign up. The
code is also used to uniquely identify the promotion that the
247

=== PAGE 252 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
Attribute Function
referral activities of advocates and their referred party belong to.
Since the referral code consists of the promotion, it’s easy to identify
how promotions are performing.
After you enter a promotion code and move to the next step of the
guided flow, you can't change the code.
Promotion page URL The URL is used to create the unique referral links for the advocates
who join the promotion. The URL that you specify is suffixed with
the advocate’s unique referral code.
Referral promotion template
The promotion template that you want to base your promotion on.
The promotion's template decides whom the promotion rewards,
the stage at which the rewards are provided. It decides whether you
can select rewards for both advocates and their referred party,
either advocates or their party, or none of them.
You can use an active template to build your promotion. After you
select a template and move to the next step of the guided flow, you
can't change the promotion's template.
11.. On the Promotions related list of your referral program, click New Referral Promotion.
22.. Define primary details of your promotion, click Save & Next.
33.. Define the rewards and audience, click Save & Next.
44.. Review the summary and click Done.
Rewards and Audience
In the second step of the guided flow, select the promotion’s rewards, limits, and target audience.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS

Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing

Rewards
The promotion template that you select for a promotion decides the rewards and at which stage the
248

=== PAGE 253 ===
Referral Marketing Design a Referral Program
rewards are provided. If the promotion template rewards both advocates and their referred party, then
you can select the voucher definitions or extended reward definitions you want to use to issue the
rewards. You can offer the same or different vouchers and extended rewards to advocates and their
referred parties.
If the promotion's template rewards either advocates or their referred party, then you can only select a
reward for whom the promotion template rewards. If the promotion's template doesn't reward anyone,
you can't select a reward in the Referral Promotion guided flow.
Tip Before you create a promotion, add the voucher definitions and extended reward definition on
the referral program page for the vouchers and extended rewards that you want to offer advocates
and their referred party.
Limits
To stay within the budget of the referral promotion and to ensure that there aren’t fraudulent referrals,
you can set limits for advocates. If a promotion template doesn't reward advocates, then you can add
limits for advocates of promotions that use the template.
Limit Type Purpose
Reward limit
Limit for the number of times an advocate can be rewarded for
successful referrals. The limit can be set for a fixed duration:
•
Promotion duration—The limit is applicable for the complete
duration of the promotion. After an advocate reaches the limit,
they’re no longer rewarded for any successful referral.
•
Calendar year—The limit is applicable for a calendar year. After an
advocate reaches the limit, they aren’t rewarded for any
successful referrals during the current year. They’re again
rewarded for the successful referrals in the next year.
For example, if the promotion’s reward limit is 5 and the advocate
was already rewarded five times in 2024, they aren’t rewarded
when their sixth referral signs up in 2024. But if the referral signs
up in 2025, the advocate is rewarded.
Daily referral limit Limit the number of referrals that advocates can submit in a day.
Target Audience
You can decide the target audience of each promotion. Only advocates who are part of the promotion’s
target audience can join the promotion and refer businesses.
You can select the target audience from these options.
249

All advocates All the advocates of the referral program are the
promotion’s target audience.
Campaign members
Advocates who are members of the selected
campaign are the promotion’s target audience.
To ensure that an advocate is part of the
campaign, the advocate’s account record must be
a member of the campaign.

can go back and make the required changes.

Can I Select a Campaign That Consists of Contacts as a Promotion’s Target
Audience?
No, the target audience of a B2B referral promotion is always advocates who have a business account
record in the org. If you select a campaign to filter a promotion’s target audience, the campaign
members must be a business account.

How Activities are Tracked in B2B Referral Management
A referral promotion must track activities that advocates and their referred parties complete through
the promotion's stages. For activities in each stage, a set of records is created or updated.
Process B2B Referral Event Action
Use the Process B2B Referral Event action in Flow Builder or through Connect API to create tracking
records for referral activities that advocates and their referred party complete during the last three
stages of promotions. The action also automates the issuing of rewards after advocates and their

records are created or updated. Use the additional elements in Flow Builder to decide the eligibility
criteria for referral activities. You can also add follow-up actions after the Process B2B Referral action.
Example Flows to Track B2B Referrals Across Sales Lifecycle
Design flows that progressively track B2B referrals provided by customers and partners as referred
businesses advance through sales lifecycle stages. For example, the flow can track the progression of
referrals from lead generation to opportunity closure or from opportunity generation to first order
fulfillment. B2B Referral Management provides businesses the flexibility to plug their referral programs
in any type of B2B sales lifecyle. In this example, two reference flows are designed to visualize how
partner referrals are tracked across the referral lifecycle during the lead to opportunity sales lifecycle
and how partners are paid out for successful referrals.

Ways to Track Referral Activities
You can track referral activities with Process Referral Event action. The admin or the developer can add
the action to an existing business process. As part of this process, advocates can refer business and
referred business can become customers of the company. The action is available for admins in Flow
Builder or through Connect API and developers can access the action as an invocable action or from
Apex.

of promotions. The action also automates the issuing of rewards after advocates and their referred party
complete eligible activities. For each activity, a transaction journal is created and other records are
