Stage 3
During the first and second stages, the promotion only interacts with the advocates. In the third stage,
advocates refer . To track an advocate’s referral, define the values for these fields:
•
Event Type —Specify Refer as the event type.
•
Referral Code —Specify the code of the advocate who referred a business and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of. Separate the codes with a hyphen.
•
Activity Date Time —Specify the date and time when the referral event was completed.
•
Referral Lead ID — Specify the lead ID of the party who was referred.
260

=== PAGE 265 ===
Referral Marketing Configure Processes
Stage 4
After advocates refer the referred party in the third stage, a lead record is created for the referred party.
The lead qualifies and converted into Account and Opportunity. To track qualification of the referred
party, define the values for these fields:
•
Event Type —Specify Qualify as the event type.
•
Referral Code —Specify the code of the advocate who referred a business and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of. Separate the codes with a hyphen.
•
Activity Date Time —Specify the date and time when the business signed up.
•
Referral Account ID —Specify the ID of the referred party's account record.
Stage 5
An opportunity is considered closed or won after a referred party signs a deal with the company. To track
this successful conversion by a referred business, define the values for these fields:
•
Event Type —Specify Closure as the event type.
•
Referral Code —Specify the code of the advocate who referred a business and the code of the
promotion that the activity is a part of. Separate the codes with a hyphen.
•
Activity Date Time —Specify the date and time when the opportunity was closed or won.
•
Referral Account ID —Specify the ID of the referred party’s account record.
Important Create a custom Referral Code field on both the Lead and Opportunity objects to store
the advocate's unique referral code for the referred party. In the flow that manages advocate
referrals, use the Update Record action to add the advocate's referral code to the Lead record
created for their referral. To pass the Referral Code value from Lead to Opportunity on Lead
Conversion, map these Referral Code fields.
If you don’t want to run the action as part of a flow, you can run it as an invocable action, Connect API or
as part of an Apex class.
Tip To ensure that the Process B2B Referral Event action doesn’t create duplicate accounts for
advocates and duplicate accounts and leads for referred parties, create matching rules and
duplicate rules on the Contact and Person Account objects.

Tracking Referrals Lead Generation to Lead Qualification
Admins can create a flow that tracks B2B referrals right from inception when leads are generated from
partner referrals until the sales team qualifies the lead. A record-triggered flow with the Process B2B
Referral Event action makes sure that partners' referrals are always tracked, regardless of whether the
lead is generated from the partner portal or offline.

Rewarding Partners for Successful Referrals
Admins can create a flow that rewards partners when leads generated from their B2B referrals result in
won opportunities. A record-triggered flow with the Process B2B Referral Event action makes sure that
partners are instantly rewarded when opportunities generated from their referrals result in a positive
outcome for the sales team.

Manage a B2B Referral Program
After advocates join the brand’s referral promotion and start referring another businesses, channel
managers can track the progress of each referral.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, and Developer Editions with Referral Marketing
Available in: Enterprise, Performance, and Unlimited Editions with Partner Ecosystem Management -
Members or Partner Ecosystem Management - Login. Learn more about Referral Marketing with Partner
Ecosystem management.
Manage Advocates
After a brand launches its referral promotion, channel managers can review the details of the
advocates who are part of the referral program and can add advocates to referral promotions.
Manage Activities
While channel managers review the performance of a referral program and its promotions, they can
review the activities completed by advocates and their referred parties.
Track Advocate Count for Promotions
When an advocate joins a promotion, a Loyalty Program Member Promotion record is automatically
created to track their participation. From the Loyalty Program Member Promotion related list on a
promotion, channel managers can track the count of advocates who have joined the promotion, the
active advocate count, and their details. channel managers can use a promotion's advocate count as a
key performance indicator of the promotion.
Track Referrals
Referral records help channel managers track the progress of an advocate’s referral. When an
advocate’s referral progresses across the promotion stages, the Referral record is also updated to the
current stage.
Track Issued Vouchers
Vouchers issued to advocates are associated with the advocate's loyalty program member record.
Channel managers can keep track of the vouchers issued to an advocate by viewing their loyalty
program member record.
Track Issued Extended Rewards
Extended rewards issued to advocates are associated with the advocate's account and extended
rewards issued to referred parties are associated with the referred party's account. channel managers
can keep a track of the extended rewards issued to a person by viewing their account.
View Promotion Configuration

View the detailed configuration of a referral promotion with one click. Users with read-only access to

promotion details and determine the changes they want to make without deactivating the promotion.

You can review these key details in a Referral record:
•
Referrer—The account of the advocate.
•
Referred Party—The lead or account record of the referred party.
•
Promotion—The promotion as part of which the advocate referred the referred party.
•
Opportunity—The opportunity created from the referral.
•
Current Promotion Stage—The stage that the referral is at currently. The stage changes as the referral
progresses through the various promotion stages.
11.. On the Promotions related list of your referral program, click the promotion whose referral you want to
view.
22.. Click Referrals.
33.. Click the name of the referral that you want to view.
